Shi Cantang, the Bombing Suspect of the First Through Train to Shenyang from Beiping, Sentenced to Death 60

His Demeanor Was Calm Before the Execution, and Spectators Pitied Him

The Zhengyi Assassination Group Was Headed by Shi Cantang

Five Suspects Sentenced to Imprisonment

Beiping Correspondence: At 8:45 a.m. on July 1, the first direct through train to Shenyang from Beiping departed from Beiping. At 1:20 p.m. that afternoon, a violent explosive device exploded in the third-class carriage near Chadian Station, resulting in the deaths of dozens of innocent passengers, with both deaths and injuries. After the incident, the authorities ordered their subordinates to strictly apprehend the main culprits who deliberately sabotaged the railway. As a result, the Third Regiment of the Central Military Police and the Beiping Public Security Bureau arrested five people, including Shi Cantang, Cao Wensheng, Pan Jun, Tang Pu, and Yuan Binxia. After investigation, Shi confessed to being the mastermind behind the incident, and the rest were suspects. The military branch sentenced Shi to capital punishment in accordance with the "Law for Punishing Acts Endangering the Republic of China". This morning (the 6th) at 9:30 a.m., Shi was escorted to Tianqiao and executed by shooting. The details of the incident are recorded below.

A Glimpse of the Execution: The Third Regiment of the Central Military Police this morning (the 6th) at 9:40 a.m. escorted Shi Cantang, the main culprit of the Chadian train bombing, from the regiment headquarters in Qianliang Hutong. Led by Regiment Deputy Yuan Jiapei, a platoon of military police officers drove in two new-style purple cars to the Tianqiao execution ground to carry out the execution. Because the case was extremely secret beforehand, few people knew about it. It was not until the police of the Outer Fifth District and the security police of the Fourth Team were on alert at Erdaotan that merchants and residents near Tianqiao began to gather at the execution ground to watch. At 9:20 a.m., more than 40 central military police officers arrived in advance by car to guard the area and drive away the spectators, which was even more serious than the situation of previous executions of criminals. The soldiers and police held guns and live ammunition in their hands, ready to shoot. At about 10 o'clock, a 1934 new purple car and a green car drove to the execution ground. The first to get out of the car were the military police, and finally, the train bomber Shi Cantang was taken out of the purple car. Shi was about twenty years old, with slicked-back hair, wearing a moon-white gown and Western-style trousers. From a distance, he looked like a handsome young man. After the criminal got out of the car, two military police officers held his arms on the left and right. Shi's demeanor was calm. On the way, he nodded and smiled slightly at the onlookers on the left and right. The onlookers all sighed with regret. Suddenly, they heard the supervising officer Yuan Jiapei shouting "Stop!" The criminal Shi knelt down facing south. After three gunshots, he was lying in a pool of blood. Later, because Shi's body was still shaking, the executing military police fired another shot at his body before he died completely. Shi's body was then buried by laborers in a mass grave outside Yongdingmen.

Recalling the Train Bombing: The through train to Shenyang from Beiping began operation on July 1 this year. The first train departing from Beiping included three first-class carriages, one second-class carriage, four third-class carriages, one guard car, and one baggage car, all of which were rolling stock from the Beining Railway, hauled by locomotive number 2189. The train captain was Zhou Dechang, the guard car attendant was Song Ziguang, the ticket inspectors were Wang Wenwei, Li Yufeng, and Liu Zhenze. On that day, the passengers departing from Beiping included 73 third-class passengers and 2 second-class passengers. At 1:20 p.m., when passing near Chadian Station, the second third-class car behind the locomotive suddenly exploded with a loud bang, and the tragedy began. Five male and female passengers died on the spot, and 27 were slightly or seriously injured. The next day, leaflets were found in Beiping, stating the motives for the train bombing, and some people indirectly warned the news media not to speak for the officials. After the police and military police authorities were ordered to strictly apprehend the culprits, Li Cantang and others were successively arrested on September 2. Shi was sentenced to death as the mastermind. Shi was from Liyang, Jiangsu, and was only in his early twenties. A few months ago, the author who used the pen name "Moron" in the supplements of various newspapers in Beiping was this gentleman.

The Course of Solving the Case: After Shi was executed, the authorities announced the course of solving the case as follows: (1) Previously, the Third Regiment of the Military Police arrested Cao Wensheng, a member of the "Zhengyi Assassination Group," and several suspects, including Pan Jun, Yuan Baoxia, and Tang Pu, in this city, and seized documents and explosives from the assassination group. During the interrogation, they learned that the Chadian train bombing was carried out by Shi Cantang, the leader of the assassination group. The Third Regiment of the Military Police then carried out extensive investigations and arrested Shi Cantang on September 2. After interrogation, Shi Cantang directly admitted that the "Zhengyi Assassination Group" was organized by him, and that the Chadian train bombing was carried out by him personally. The "Letter to Chadian Station" and the "Letter to the People of the Whole Country" were also written by him; (2) Shi Cantang learned that the through train to Shenyang from Beiping was about to be implemented, so he planned the train bombing plan, put a large amount of explosives into a thermos bottle to avoid inspection, and took it to Tianjin on June 30. After installing the explosive detonator, he took the first through train to Shenyang from Beiping on July 1 from Tianjin, and then placed the thermos bottle filled with explosives in the third-class carriage. Shi got off the train at Tanggu Station and returned to Beiping. When the through train arrived at Chadian Station, it was bombed; (3) After the Third Regiment of the Military Police learned the truth of the case, it reported the results of the interrogation to the military branch for review, considering the seriousness of the case. Now the military branch believes that at a time when the local area is unstable, Shi Cantang dared to organize an assassination group and use explosives to destroy railway transportation, resulting in the tragic deaths of many passengers. He is extremely illegal and has been sentenced to death to Shi Cantang to warn others. The members of his assassination group, Cao Wensheng, etc., were also sentenced to imprisonment according to law. Yesterday (the 6th) morning at 10 o'clock, the Second Regiment of the Military Police took Shi Cantang to verify his identity and sent Wu Tuan to escort him to the Tianqiao execution ground to carry out the shooting.

Proclamation of the Military Branch: Proclamation of the Beiping Branch of the Military Commission of the National Government, Zhengfa Zi No. 2, regarding the proclamation: It is reported that the Third Regiment of the Military Police has successively arrested Shi Cantang, the perpetrator of the Chadian train bombing on the Beining Road, and five suspects, Cao Wensheng, Pan Jun, Tang Pu, and Yuan Baoxia. After interrogation, it has been clarified that the perpetrator Shi Cantang is the mastermind and perpetrator of the Chadian train bombing, and all the bombing plans were conceived by him, and he issued the "Letter to Chadian Station" and the "Letter to the People of the Whole Country", which is true. Considering that it was the beginning of the operation of the through train to Shenyang from Beiping, the perpetrator Shi Cantang recklessly used explosives to destroy the railway, resulting in the injury and death of many passengers. Such disturbance of public order is extremely sinful and should be punished with the death penalty in accordance with Article 5, Paragraph 3 of the "Emergency Law for Punishing Acts Endangering the Republic of China". Cao Wensheng, Pan Jun, Tang Pu, Yuan Baoxia, and the other four have also been sentenced to fixed-term imprisonment according to law, and handed over to the prison for execution and temporary custody for further investigation. In addition to taking the perpetrator Shi Cantang to the execution ground to verify his identity and sending personnel to escort him to the execution ground to carry out the shooting, in order to uphold the law and warn others, this proclamation is hereby issued to inform all the people. Chairman Jiang Zhongzheng, acting He Yingqin, October 6, 23rd year of the Republic of China (6th).

Notorious Bandit Executed in Eastern Shandong 61

Bandit Leader Wang Zimei and Four Others

Repeatedly Kidnapped in Various Counties in Jiaodong

Qingdao Correspondence: Bandit leaders Wang Cheng from Laiyang County and Pingdu County, previously gathered dozens of people and kidnapped and extorted ransoms in Pingdu, Laiyang, Jimo, Zhucheng, Rizhao, and Haiyang, and cruelly killed innocent people. There were numerous cases and repeated attempts to arrest them failed. The bandits recently sneaked into Qingdao City again, intending to engage in activities. Due to improper secrecy, they were arrested by the Public Security Bureau and the Marine Corps one after another and sentenced to death. It is found that bandit Wang is from Laiyang County, 23 years old. Two years ago, he carried a handgun and sneaked into Qingdao, and flaunted his wealth in Pingkangli and various theaters, attracting attention. He was arrested by the Public Security Bureau and sent to the court. At that time, because the bandit changed his name and refused to tell the truth, the court only sentenced him to six months imprisonment according to the regulations for banning the private possession of military weapons. After being released from prison, the bandit resumed his old business and committed numerous crimes in Jimo and Pingdu counties. Last month, he sneaked into Qingdao again and gathered party members, intending to kidnap people in Laiyang County, and purchased handguns, leather bags, and bullet belts in Qingdao in advance for use in the countryside. Unexpectedly, due to improper secrecy, the Third Fleet Command and the Public Security Bureau learned about it. When the bandit passed through Liuting, the Second Battalion of the Marine Corps detained the car, and bandit Wang and his accomplice Gan Xixian were arrested on the spot, and gun bags and other items were found. Gong Shunyi, a bandit collaborator, was also arrested east of Jimo City, and a handgun and a large number of bullets were found in Gong's home. At the same time, the Public Security Bureau also sent police to the station and pier to conduct a strict search, and arrested four bandits, Wang Qingfu, Wang Xinxi, Lu Defeng, and Zhang Yuandong, because they knew that the bandit leader had been arrested and planned to take trains and ships to flee to other ports. Another escaped bandit, Sun Kuiwu, fled to Laiyang County and was arrested by the garrison. The Qingdao Public Security Bureau sent personnel to bring bandit Sun back to the city for repeated interrogation. The bandits confessed to the kidnapping. The Pingdu and Laiyang County governments both sent official documents proving the bandits' crimes in their respective counties, requesting that they be sentenced to capital punishment to uphold the law. Subsequently, the Qingdao Naval Office sent personnel to interrogate, recorded the confessions and reported them to the Weihai Third Fleet Command, which pronounced the sentence on October 27. Except for Zhang Yuandong, Lu Shunyi, and Gan Xixian, whose circumstances were relatively minor and sentenced to imprisonment, and sent to Licun Fifth Prison for execution, Wang Chengmei, Wang Qingfu, Sun Kuiwu, Wang Xinxi, and Lu Defeng, repeatedly kidnapped people for ransom and committed heinous crimes, and were sentenced to death together. After receiving the order, the Qingdao Naval Office, together with the Public Security Bureau, sent military police to escort the five criminals, Wang Chengmei and others, to the No. 5 Battery execution ground this morning (the 5th) at 9 a.m. to carry out the shooting. At the End of the Autumn Flood Season, the Yellow River Surges Again 62

Water Level Exceeds This Year's Maximum Flood Level

Kaifeng Correspondence: As the end of the autumn flood season approaches, there has been excessive rainfall in the upper reaches of the Yellow River. On the 2nd and 3rd, water levels were reported to be rising everywhere. The flow rate at Tongguan reached 10,000 cubic meters per second, and on the 3rd, the water level exceeded this year's maximum flood level. Chen Ruzhen, director of the Provincial River Affairs Bureau, together with technician Tao Shuceng, went to Liuyuan, Heigang, Zhongmu, Zhengzhou, and Rongze on the morning of the 3rd to inspect the engineering defenses. They returned to the province at 6 p.m. and discussed the situation of each project as follows: (1) The water level at Rongze Flood Control is 1.07 meters higher than the flood on August 11. The eighth revetment of the first embankment was eroded at the bottom and the front eyebrow collapsed. The Chief of the Shangnansu Sub-bureau is leading workers to throw stones for emergency protection, which is expected to be safe; (2) The western section of the Zhenshang Flood Control, near the large levee south of the river, is still stable, but there is very little stone stored on the embankment; (3) The sixth revetment of the eighth embankment of the Zhongmu Shang Flood Control had previously collapsed at the top of the levee, but has been stabilized with emergency protection. On the 3rd, the embankment root was disturbed again by two zhang. Overseeing the workers to carry out emergency protection has already been dispatched; (4) There is no danger to the western section of the Heigang Project as the levee is moving, but the levee in the eastern section is moving south. An order to hire workers to throw stones to protect the bank has already been issued; (5) The southern enclosure of the Liuyuankou River is collapsing very rapidly. The top of the first embankment of the eleventh stronghold is being hit by a large levee, which is extremely critical. An order has been issued to the Chief of the Xinan Liu Sub-bureau to lead workers to guard it day and night. Furthermore, it was reported on the 3rd from Shangbei that the western cliff stone dam of the Wuzhi Flood Control was slightly disturbed and emergency repairs are underway, and the water level outside the old channel entrance of Nan Lanfeng has risen by six centimeters, but all projects are still stable. The engineering situation in Xibei, according to the Xibei Sub-bureau, was reported by telegram at night that the river pattern of the nineteenth stronghold in the Kaifeng Xishun is constantly changing, and a large reflux has been discovered at the top of the fifth stronghold, which is flowing fiercely towards the west. On the 1st, the embankment's base here was disturbed by two zhang and five chi, and the bottom of the eighth levee was disturbed by a stone and was removed by four zhang, and the ninth levee was disturbed and removed by two zhang and five chi. At the same time, the straw bags at the bottom of the first embankment of the twentieth stronghold were disturbed and removed by five zhang, and the straw bags at the bottom of the second embankment were disturbed and removed by seven zhang. The River Affairs Bureau, upon receiving the report, has sent the chief of the engineering department, together with the Magistrate of Kaifeng County, across the river on the afternoon of the 3rd to assist in the emergency protection in the area of Chenqiao, and has telegraphed the sub-bureaus and the Hua County Laoanti Engineering Office to make every effort to protect it day and night, and has reported it to the Provincial Government for review. Huang Yaoting, a Prominent Figure in the Beiping Pawnshop Industry, Commits Suicide 63

Owned More Than a Dozen Pawnshops at His Peak

Suffered Social and Economic Impacts, Leading to Bankruptcy

Beiping Correspondence: Six years ago, due to the fact that the Central Government's orders were most concentrated here, many great merchants and wealthy entrepreneurs pursued one-tenth of the profits, started businesses, and held the economic reins in this five-capital city. In the past, society praised those who described their successful and wealthy attributes with their occupations, such as the Zhong Yang family, the Gong Wang family, the Huang Dang family, and the Wen Ma family. Although today many have become the decline of noble families, in the prosperous times of the Qing Dynasty, they were all like the wealthy and powerful in the capital, known to all, and enjoyed more pleasure than the emperors of the world. (The Zhong Yang family started with clocks, the Gong Wang family became wealthy by selling offerings of New Year's candies, and the Wen Ma family in Qinlao Hutong made their fortune by selling cultural relics, antiques, and calligraphy and paintings. The Huang Dang family specialized in clothing pawnshops. In Beiping's customs, those who associated their occupation with their surname to form a nickname were definitely the giants in this occupation. The meaning is like the American titles of "Oil King," "Car King," and "News King," which are the same as their honor and prominence. Unexpectedly, this morning (the 4th) at 10 o'clock, Huang Yaoting, the owner of the so-called "Huang Dang family," the giant in the pawnshop industry, suddenly committed suicide. This is truly the sad news of the near decline of the old feudal social property class. At the same time, it can also be seen that the severe changes in the Beiping economy have presented an irresistible stage. The reporter believes that the suicide of the host,

Posthumous Photograph of Huang Yaoting, Leader of the Pawn Industry in Beiping, Nicknamed "Huang of the Pawnshops" 64

To represent the influential members of the wealthy society of the old capital and (leader of the pawn industry), and as this matter is also good material for those studying social problems, we made a special trip to visit and obtained the details of the process and the inside story as follows:

Huang Yaoting's ancestral residence was at No. 46, Jiudaowan Hutong, Beixinqiao, Beiping. Since the庚子 Boxer Rebellion, he started his business in the pawn industry. At its peak, he controlled more than a dozen pawnshops. Therefore, his family was known for its wealth. Recently, since the government moved south and commerce declined, the pawnshops owned by the Huang family could initially barely support two or three. However, in recent months, they have all closed down simultaneously, and even the livelihood of his family has fallen into poverty. Mr. Huang is already sixty years old and has been accustomed to a wealthy life. The sudden blow was unbearable. His temperament was also that of a cautious businessman who was not good at socializing. As his livelihood became strained, his social interactions became even more difficult. His son, who originally held a minor position in the military, was recently laid off. His granddaughter, whom he used to cherish like a pearl, was also expelled from Chongci Girls' High School for failing to pay her tuition. His son, named Wanduo, was already unemployed at home. As a result, father and son often had arguments. Huang, with his stubborn and old-fashioned mind, believed that his personal future had no hope due to family poverty, business failure, and his son's filial impiety. Dwelling on the past and present, he resolved to commit suicide. Yesterday (the 3rd), Mr. Huang went out and privately purchased a bottle of sleeping pills. That night, he locked himself in his room and took them. By this morning, his family was still unaware. His wife, Zhao, got up first as usual and took care of everything. When his granddaughter, Xiguang, got up, Mr. Huang was still in bed. Fortunately, Xiguang had a keen sense and thought that her grandfather usually went out for a walk at 8:00 AM. Why was he still in bed so late today? There must be a reason. So she went to her grandfather's bedroom and called him three times, but there was no response. She pushed him with her hand, but he did not move. Xiguang suddenly felt that something was wrong and cried loudly for her family to come and investigate together. They discovered the empty bottle of sleeping pills that Mr. Huang had taken. It was then determined that the head of the family had indeed committed suicide by taking poison, without any doubt. His son immediately reported to the Third District, Twelfth Section of the Public Security Bureau in the inner city and carried Mr. Huang to the nearby Daoji Hospital for emergency treatment. By 5:00 PM, he still had a slight breath, but the doctor said that he was too old and there was absolutely no hope for recovery. When the reporter was writing this manuscript late at night, he called the hospital again and was told that Mr. Huang was still unconscious and unable to speak. Based on common sense, it is feared that this pawn industry magnate, who represents the wealthy merchant class of the old capital, has no hope of survival. Miss Huang Xiguang, Huang's granddaughter, told the reporter, "I am seventeen years old and used to study at Chongci High School. Recently, I had to drop out due to family poverty. My grandfather's death was purely due to business failure, family unrest, and the inability to make a living, which led him to take this unfortunate path of no return. I regret being born into a wealthy family and not being able to relieve my elderly relative's worries with a skill. I feel ashamed and have no interest in life." The reporter visited his residence during the day. The flowers and branches were flourishing, and the utensils were clean. However, the house was in a state of disarray, truly a vivid and tragic symbol of the decline of a once-prominent family. (4th)

They hired workers and purchased materials to build a large building. The society members were divided into permanent and ordinary types. There was an enthusiastic response to joining. Then, the directors and supervisors were elected, and the meeting was adjourned after a photograph was taken.

Four Robberies in a Row Near Tinglin 66

In the Xiawutu area of Huangku Township, Tinglin, at about 11:00 PM the day before yesterday, more than a dozen armed bandits suddenly broke into the home of farmer Yu Chunqiao. Yu Wensheng and Yu Yu-shi, who lived with him, were all locked in one room. They were forced to hand over money and belongings, and Yu Wensheng was beaten. Then, they searched the house and fled with their loot. They then went to the homes of He Bozhou and Gu Awu in the same area one after another to search and rob. Gu Awu resisted slightly and was beaten and injured by the bandits. He was robbed of 85 yuan in silver, clothing, and other items. He Bozhou's home was robbed of 5 yuan in silver, silver ornaments, and clothing. Yu Chunqiao's home lost three quilts, many items of clothing, several bolts of calico, and a pair of silver bracelets. Yu Wensheng's home was robbed of 15 yuan in silver and five bolts of cloth. Four robberies in a row in one night show the rampant nature of banditry.

Jiading

Civilians in Fangtai Recover a Bandit Boat 67

In the Beishagang Bridge area of Fangtai, on the afternoon of the 4th, seven awning boats arrived, winding through the small rivers in the countryside. The wife of Wu Heting from Zhongmi Village saw several strong men on the boats landing and stealing chickens and ducks in the bamboo forest during the day. She immediately shouted to stop them, but the bandits ignored her. She urgently sounded the gong to raise the alarm. The bandits then tried to snatch the gong away. When neighboring villagers heard the alarm and responded, they hurriedly boarded their boats and headed west. Passing through Shaojia Village, Chen Ruisheng caught sight of them putting dozens of stolen chickens into cloth bags and sinking them into the river with stones. Hundreds of civilians chased them to Sanliqiao. The Fangtai branch of the Public Security Bureau also heard the news and sent police to rush to the scene. The bandits then surrendered. Six bandit boats and more than 30 male and female bandits were captured and escorted to the county government by the Public Security Bureau branch on the 5th for interrogation. As for the one boat that escaped, some said that it had 12 bandits on board and was carrying weapons. It is said that these bandits belonged to the Shuihuo Gang (Water and Fire Gang), and thefts of large numbers of chickens and ducks by them in various places have been heard of from time to time.

Continuous Burglaries in the City 68

The Zhou Shugu warehouse in Hulong Street in the city suffered a burglary last month, losing more than 10,000 yuan in banknotes and silver. The county government ordered a deadline for solving the case, but it has not been solved yet. The suspects arrested by the water police have been interrogated and found to be unrelated to the case. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 5th, a traveler passing through the Meicun Bridge area outside Pingmen suddenly encountered five bandits who blocked the road and robbed him. Fortunately, the traveler shouted loudly for help, and the railway police heard the sound and rushed to the scene. The bandits then fled, and the traveler was not harmed. Unexpectedly, at 8:30 PM on the evening of the 6th, the Yongxinhe thread and rope shop at No. 19, Xiaozhu Lane, Shantang Street outside 阊 Gate, was attacked by three bandits speaking with a 客家 Hakka accent, each carrying guns. They shouted to prohibit any resistance and rushed into the shop, forcing the accountant, Zhao Jinrong, to point out where the silver was hidden. They were robbed of 70 角 in small silver coins, 21 yuan in banknotes and silver, and 12.3 yuan in large silver corner bills. They disappeared quickly. After the bandits left, the owner immediately reported to the police district and detective team in charge to pursue and arrest them. That night, the detective team sent detectives to investigate in all directions, but there was no trace of them. County Magistrate Wu paid close attention to the continuous burglaries in the city. On the 7th, he strictly ordered the Public Security Bureau to arrest the main culprits in each case and punish them severely according to the law.

American Doctor Invents Tuberculosis Treatment Machine 70

The Wu County Medical Association held a meeting at the Boxi Hospital on the afternoon of the 6th. During the meeting, an American named Lan Wanyi (transliteration) gave a lecture. She has been researching tuberculosis in the United States for more than 20 years. She invented a machine based on her research findings. Within 24 hours, using a 5% liquid, it can gradually eliminate tuberculosis bacteria. She also conducted experiments with rabbits, and the results were very satisfactory. In the United States, she has cured many people with stage 4 lung disease. She was introduced to China by a friend and will continue her research at Boxi Hospital. She is confident that she has already succeeded. If so, then this machine is truly a valuable invention in medicine.

Wuxi

The Young Owner of a Brewery Flees and Attempts Suicide 71

The Luyoufeng sauce garden and brewery in this county is owned by the brothers Lu Boping and Lu Zhenxiu from this county. The business is prosperous. Therefore, there are as many as eight branches inside and outside the city. Zhenxiu's son, Jinlong, once worked at the Youcheng Silk Factory and Xinyuan Money Shop, and co-founded the Dingcheng Flour Mill in Beitang with Guo Jiliang and others. In recent years, Jinlong became obsessed with operating in the stock exchange, resulting in a loss of more than 2,000 yuan. The Dingcheng Flour Mill also went bankrupt because of it. The creditors sued the court for debt collection. Zhenxiu, Jinlong's father, found out about this and severely scolded Jinlong. In a fit of anger, Jinlong left home with his wife, Xu Yufen, in November of last year and stayed at the Park Hotel. Recently, his financial difficulties have become more severe, and he is surrounded by enemies. Unable to maintain his livelihood, he had thoughts of ending his life. He tried to drown himself in the river near the Beitang Fudian Temple. Fortunately, he was rescued. However, although he could not die, he still did not return to his hotel. His wife, not seeing her husband, returned home, knowing that something had changed. She searched everywhere and found Jinlong's sworn brother, Yao Yimin, and saw five suicide notes from Jinlong to his uncle Wuxiu, aunt Ding Lu, wife Xu Yufen, sworn brother Yao Yimin, and other relatives and friends. The notes stated that he would throw himself into the vast ocean and instructed his wife to take care of their children and repay her in the next life. The Lu family is now extremely anxious and is searching everywhere. It is unknown whether he can return safely.

Three Burglaries in the Second and Third Districts 72

Hui Mo-biao, a resident of Zhoujing Lane North, Jinhua Lane, in the second district (Jingyun City) of the county, has a modest family fortune. He runs the Wanshunyi Southern Goods Store under Jingqiao in the Southern Gate. He has three sons and one daughter. At about 11:00 PM the night before last, five or six bandits suddenly came to the Hui family, entered through a hole dug in the empty house next door, and searched arbitrarily, each carrying a pistol and iron shovel, with painted faces. Hui's second son, A-er, heard the bandits' accent and knew that they were all locals. One of the bandits was a fellow villager named Hua Rongchu, whom A-er recognized. The bandit knew that things were not good and swung his axe at A-er. Fortunately, he dodged quickly, and only his right forehead was slightly injured. The robbery lasted for an hour before they left with their loot and fled towards the railway. Afterwards, upon inspection, it was discovered that gold, silver jewelry, clothing, and other items worth about 100 yuan had been stolen. The next day, A-er came to the city, intending to report the robbery at home to his father in the store. Unexpectedly, he ran into the bandit Hua Rongchu on a narrow road under Qingming Bridge. He immediately dragged him into the Third Branch Bureau, transferred him to the General Bureau, and then transferred him to the county government. Clerk Yu opened the court for interrogation. The criminal Hua confessed to the robbery and was ordered to be handcuffed and detained. Also, the family of Pan Rongquan in Pan Lane, the 267th and 268th districts of the Third District, was visited by five bandits the night before last. The loss from the robbery in the room was small. Because the bandits were not satisfied with their loot, they went to Zhang Gensheng's home in Zhang Lane, the 267th and 268th districts, to search and rob. They were robbed of more than 200 yuan in cash and clothing, for a total loss of more than 300 yuan.

Changzhou

County-wide Registration of Opium Addicts Concluded 73

The Wuyi County Anti-Smoking Association has been conducting the registration of opium addicts since its establishment. The deadline was the 30th of last month. However, because most of the district offices had not completed the follow-up procedures, a five-day extension was granted. As of the 6th, all reports have been compiled. The County Anti-Smoking Association has completed the calculation and statistics. There are 752 first-class addicts, 3,638 second-class addicts, for a total of 4,390 addicts. County Magistrate Hou estimated that there were about 15,000 opium addicts in the county during the initial investigation. Now, only one-third have registered. Some have quit voluntarily due to strict anti-smoking measures, but many have avoided registration. He has telegraphed the Provincial Anti-Smoking Association to ask for instructions on how to deal with this in the future.

Cloth Shop Clears 300,000 Yuan in Debt 77

The Kaitai Cloth Shop in front of the Gulou in Hangzhou has been in business for more than 80 years and has had annual surpluses. Manager Li Jintang has been in charge of the shop for 40 years since his father passed away. Therefore, his private property and accumulated assets are extremely rich. He also serves as the president of the Hangzhou Zhongnan Bank. This year, due to difficulties in collecting debts in the Upper River area, he suddenly entrusted a lawyer to announce the clearing of debts, totaling more than 100,000 yuan owed to various banks and money shops (only a few hundred yuan to Zhongnan) and more than 200,000 yuan to depositors. When depositors heard the news, they were greatly alarmed. The Public Security Bureau also found that the shop's accounts were inaccurate, so they summoned Li to the bureau for questioning at the request of the creditors and sent police to monitor him. The municipal government believed that this matter had a significant impact on society. In addition to ordering the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to investigate and order the shop to handle it carefully, yesterday, the Social Affairs Section summoned Li Jintang to the government to inquire about the truth and ordered him to be responsible for continuing to maintain and restore business. On the one hand, he was ordered to continue to maintain and restore business and gradually repay the depositors. It is heard that the acceptance of deposits from shops is considered inappropriate and has many abuses, and it is planned to find a way to ban it.

Suicide Due to Business Failure 78

Liu Fangquan, the owner of the Yichang Hotel at No. 8, Taipingqiao District Street, Hangzhou, 33 years old, from Zhuji, had exhausted his capital due to sluggish business. Yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, he suddenly had thoughts of ending his life. While his wife was out buying tea, he locked the door, went upstairs, and hanged himself. It was reported to the police station, which forwarded it to the court to send someone to examine it and confirmed that it was true, and filled out the form for coffin burial.

Liu Weichi Talks About the Recent Work of the Ministry of Industry 82

Xinsheng News reported that Liu Weichi, Vice Minister of the Ministry of Industry, came to Shanghai on official business a few days ago. He has been staying in Shanghai for some time and has not yet returned to Beijing. A reporter from Xinsheng News visited him at his private residence yesterday and was received. He talked in detail about the recent efforts of the Ministry of Industry in various undertakings and the current implementation situation. The details are recorded below:

Cotton Suppression The Ministry of Industry believes that in the past, China's cotton was not only used for domestic consumption but also for export. However, most merchants still only care about profit and do not consider the quality of cotton, so they add water and adulterate it. The Ministry of Industry entrusted the Commodity Inspection Bureau to handle this, but it was only for exports. Now, the establishment of the suppression office is for both exports and domestic sales. The Shanghai Suppression Office has started working on the 1st. It can be formally established within this week. The Ministry of Industry is negotiating with various provinces on the establishment of cotton adulteration and water addition suppression offices in various provinces. It is planned to first establish them in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Hebei, Shandong, Henan, and other provinces. Hebei is already in progress and can be established first. The director will be concurrently held by the Director of the Construction Department of the province.

Various Manufacturing Plants The second thing I talked about was the various manufacturing plants planned by the Ministry of Industry. In addition to the alcohol plant, which was requested by overseas Chinese Huang Jiangquan to jointly operate with the Ministry of Industry, it was approved. The construction of the plant is progressing very quickly, and it is expected to ship goods next month. In addition, the plans for the newsprint plant have been prepared. The business side will invest 1.2 million, and the government will invest 4 million. The government's funds will be allocated and borrowed from the British Boxer Indemnity Fund. The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund Conference was held in Beijing the day before yesterday. This should be decided. However, the water dam project of the paper mill needs time for surveying, but there are no other problems. In addition, the Ministry of Industry plans to set up an artificial silk manufacturing plant, but it is limited by funds. The report that silk merchants from Jiangsu and Zhejiang went to the Ministry of Industry to ask for instructions to jointly operate with the government is not true.

Relief for National Coal Recently, the Ministry of Industry plans to convene a national coal relief conference. This matter has been brewing for a long time. Because without a complete and unified plan for the relief of national coal, it cannot be put into effect. Although several large domestic coal mining companies have found ways to save themselves, it is not a universal and permanent plan after all. The Ministry of Industry has considered this matter again and again and has also sent people to various places to inspect it separately. Now the inspection reports are being compiled and will be submitted for reference at the conference. The meeting can be held this month.

Production Conference Regarding the National Production Conference, this was requested by the industrial circles in various places to be convened by the Ministry of Industry. The purpose is to enable the leaders and experts of the industrial circles in various places to gather together, exchange opinions, and discuss the progress of industrial production together. This meeting was originally planned to be held in July, but it was suspended due to the hot weather. Recently, it is planned to be held in November. However, the specific date is currently undecided.

Pan Yangyao Talks About the National People's Welcome of Domestic Goods 83

Provinces Are Establishing Domestic Goods Companies One After Another

Shenshi News reported that since our country's domestic goods industry and commerce have cooperated closely with the financial community and actively implemented production and sales cooperation, the future of domestic goods is gradually becoming optimistic. A reporter from Shenshi News visited Mr. Pan Yangyao, who is familiar with the domestic goods industry. According to him, our country's domestic goods industry had a boom once during the May 30th period. In addition, it has been oppressed by the massive dumping of foreign goods and cannot raise its head. In recent years, some of our people have gradually become aware of this, and domestic goods manufacturers are also trying to promote domestic products. On the one hand, they are cooperating closely with the financial community. At the same time, manufacturers and merchants are carrying out production and sales cooperation, and the results are very good. Now, the China National Goods Company of the China Production and Marketing Cooperation Association and the National National Goods Company Office have been established in Chongqing, Chengdu, and other places. In addition, Changsha, Wenzhou, Zhenjiang, Fuzhou, Shaanxi, Hankou, Nanchang, and other places have also been roughly prepared and can be formally established on a regular basis. Merchants from various provinces, such as Gansu and Yunnan, have also sent many letters welcoming domestic goods to go for promotion. It can be seen that the psychology of our people has changed, and the future of the domestic goods industry is very optimistic.

Japanese Coal Imports Have Decreased Significantly Since September 18th 84

Chinese Merchants and Factories Have Mostly Switched to Domestic Coal

Datong News reported that before September 18th, almost all the coal used by factories in this port was Japanese coal. As a result, the annual import volume of Japanese coal was extremely large. After September 18th, manufacturers, compelled by righteous indignation, unanimously switched to domestic coal. As a result, immature domestic coal and other types of coal have gradually developed. A reporter from Datong News learned from the Coal Industry Association that before September 18th, the Japanese coal used by various factories totaled more than 20 million yuan annually. Now, except for the factories established and manufactured by Japanese merchants in our country, the remaining Chinese merchants and factories have almost completely switched to domestic coal. According to the latest survey statistics, the monthly import of Japanese coal is about 450,000 tons, worth about 650,000 yuan in national currency. Calculating the whole year, it is only about 8 million yuan, a decrease of four-fifths compared to before. This is indeed a very good phenomenon.

Japanese Typhoon Affects Foreign Trade 86

But in August, Trade with China still Had a Surplus of 5.5 Million

According to the Japanese Shanghai Daily News on the 7th, a telegram from the Tokyo Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the Japanese Commercial Counselor in this port stated that the damage caused by the wind and flood disaster in Kansai has had little impact on export industries. However, ship traffic in Osaka Port has been disrupted. Many goods in the two ports of Osaka and Kobe cannot be shipped out, and many contracts have been terminated. The biggest damage is to glass products, bicycles, electric bulbs, etc. Other enameled ironware and processed cotton cloth have also been hit considerably. It will take two months or so to restore the original state. On the other hand, among the imported goods, cotton has also suffered greatly. The damage to the quality is as high as 150,000 bales, of which 70% can still be used. Wool, raw rubber, dyes, etc. have also been damaged to varying degrees. Therefore, exports in September were 171 million, but due to the suspension of exports from Osaka Port, imports exceeded exports by 15 million. From January onwards, the cumulative excess of imports over exports was 102 million, an increase of 47% compared to the previous year. In trade with China in mid-August, exports were 14 million and exports exceeded imports by 5.57 million. From January onwards, the cumulative excess of exports over imports was 12.3 million.

Preventing Juxingcheng from Borrowing Money from the British 87

Sichuan Fellow-Provincials Association Passed a Resolution at Yesterday's Meeting

Guowen News Agency reports that the Shanghai Sichuan Fellow-Provincials Association held a regular meeting at its office on Jiujiang Road yesterday at 1:00 PM. All committee members attended, chaired by Wu Youdan. The following important matters were resolved: (1) Regarding the Juxingcheng Bank's use of foreign capital, this association, out of prudence, had previously formed a treaty research committee to meticulously study the contract signed between the bank and the British. The treaty committee has now concluded that it is inappropriate and requested a letter be sent to advise against proceeding. The detailed report was presented to the meeting. It was resolved that, considering the current tense military situation in Sichuan due to the suppression of the Red Army, the people are in a state of uncertainty, and all production and construction are temporarily out of the question. There is no need to borrow money. A letter should be sent immediately requesting the cessation of the process and the cancellation of the agreement. (2) To maintain the current financial situation in Sichuan, it was resolved to investigate and petition the central government to confiscate funds that have recently been brought to Shanghai by active-duty military personnel and their affiliated financial staff from Sichuan Province. These funds should be used to supplement the expenses for suppressing the Red Army. This resolution was passed. (3) It was resolved to petition the government to strictly prevent the departure of family members of Sichuan military officers from Sichuan via the Yichang and Hankou routes during the tense suppression of the Red Army. Furthermore, active-duty military personnel in Sichuan should be informed that they must not use excuses to evade duty or transport their families out of Sichuan, as this would hinder the suppression of the Red Army and disrupt public morale. Violators should be punished as deserters and subject to military law. This resolution was passed. (4) It was resolved to contact fellow provincials in Hankou, Nanjing, and other capital cities to form a Red Army suppression supervision group to gather relevant materials to supplement what the government may not be aware of and to supervise the Sichuan armies in their earnest suppression efforts. This resolution was passed. (5) It was resolved to send a telegram to the Ministry of Education requesting them to inform the relevant authorities of each school to waive tuition fees or seek other effective relief measures for students from Sichuan who are studying in Shanghai and facing financial difficulties due to the high exchange rate in Sichuan. This resolution was passed. The meeting was then adjourned.

According to a reporter from the Guowen News Agency, the manager of the Shanghai branch of Juxingcheng Bank stated that the bank's general manager, Yang Cansan, had telegraphed earlier, saying that the contract signed with the British to form the Lianyi Company stipulated a six-month period. If the agreement is not fulfilled within this time, it will be considered invalid. Two months have already passed since the signing of this contract. Considering the current situation in Sichuan, it will be difficult to pacify the region in a short period of time. Not only are the British unwilling to invest, but the bank is also unwilling to rashly make meaningless sacrifices and waste manpower and financial resources. Therefore, the bank had previously listed reasons and explained everything to the Shanghai Fellow-Provincials Association, and stated that it had formally declared to the British merchant that it would stop the process.

The Jiaxu Disaster Relief Association Petitions the Zhejiang Provincial Government to Quickly Allocate Large Sums of Money for Emergency Relief and Work Relief 93

Six Million for Emergency Relief, Twelve Million for Work Relief

Wang Xiaolai and Others Went to Hangzhou Yesterday Morning to Petition the Provincial Government

20 Million Yuan of New Zhejiang Provincial Public Bonds to be Used for Disaster Relief and Construction

After the Issuance of Zhejiang Local Public Bonds, Negotiations are Held with Banks Regarding Mortgages 94

Regulations Have Been Promulgated, and Public Bonds Will Be Printed

Weekly Interest Rate of Six Percent, Priced at Ninety-Eight

Weekly Interest Rate of Six Percent, Priced at Ninety-Eight

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, the regulations for the 20 million yuan Zhejiang local public bonds for the Republic of China Year 23, which were issued by the Zhejiang Provincial Government for disaster relief and other purposes, have been promulgated by the National Government. The interest rate is 6%. The Zhejiang Provincial Government has negotiated mortgages with banks in Shanghai. According to Xinsheng News Agency reporters, the situation is as follows:

Promulgation of Issuance: The regulations for the 20 million yuan public bonds issued by the Zhejiang Provincial Government for disaster relief etc. have been promulgated by the National Government. There are over fifteen articles. The weekly interest rate is 6%. According to the face value, it is issued at ninety-eight. The face value stipulates that it will be issued on October 1st. Interest will only be paid within two years from the date of issuance. Repayment of principal will begin in the third year, and principal and interest will be cleared by September 30th of the 38th year of the Republic of China. Principal will be repaid eight times a year in the 3rd and 9th months of each year through a lottery draw. Public bond denominations are divided into 10,000 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan.

Negotiating Mortgages: Although these public bonds are stipulated to be issued on October 1st, according to the general practice of issuing public bonds, the official date of sale must wait until the public bonds are printed. Alternatively, public bond subscription certificates may be issued first, and then exchanged after printing. The Zhejiang Provincial Government has negotiated public bond mortgages with banks in Shanghai and has obtained the consent of each bank. The mortgage method still needs to be further negotiated. At the same time, a fund management committee will be organized to hand over the income from various guarantee taxes designated for the principal and interest repayment fund to the fund management committee for safekeeping.

For the purpose of this, Wang Xiaolai, Chu Huiseng, Yin Zhufu, Zhang Xiaolin, Zhang Weiru, Kui Yanfang, and other members of the Shanghai Jiaxu All-Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association, took the 7:50 AM express train to Hangzhou yesterday morning to attend the Zhejiang Relief Affairs Conference and petition the provincial government to allocate 18 million yuan in work and emergency relief funds for relief. The opinions and methods obtained are as follows:

Opinions: The Jiaxu All-Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association's Proposal to the Provincial Government for the Distribution of Public Bonds

The original text states: "The 20 million yuan in disaster relief public bonds newly issued by Zhejiang Province were subject to winter telegrams from various Zhejiang fellow-provincial groups in Shanghai last month, requesting the undertaking of emergency relief and the repair of water conservancy throughout the province, and the use of work as relief, etc. Representatives were subsequently elected to petition the provincial government. This [association] has found that the drought disaster is severe, and after years of famine, and in the autumn of the collapse of rural villages, the livelihood of poor farmers has reached the end of the road and must be saved. The preparation of emergency relief is truly urgent. Work relief relates to water conservancy throughout the province, which is an essential plan for preventing future drought and flood, both fundamentally and symptomatically, and relies on large sums of money. The [association] has now drafted emergency and work relief standards for the distribution of public bonds, and humbly requests that they be examined and submitted to the Political Affairs Conference for discussion and implementation, so that millions of disaster victims may be able to survive. [We will be] endlessly grateful."

Emergency Relief: Investigate counties where there is no harvest and provide emergency relief first. According to the investigation report of the National Government's Relief Committee, the total area affected by the disaster in Zhejiang is 23,619,000 mu. Assuming that those with no harvest account for three-tenths of the total, there are 7,085,700 mu. Assuming that each disaster victim occupies 3 mu of land, the total number of disaster victims is approximately 2,361,900. Each person requires 2 dou of rice for relief, approximately 470,000 shi. Excluding the central government's exemption of taxes for purchasing foreign rice, each shi costs 7 yuan, for a total of 3,290,000 yuan. Please allocate 6 million yuan in public bonds, which, mortgaged at a 60% discount, would yield 3.6 million yuan, sufficient for purchasing rice.

Work Relief: Use local farmers to dredge the rivers, streams, ditches, and ponds in the disaster-stricken areas. This is the most essential and beneficial method of work relief in Zhejiang. The total area that should be dredged in the province has not been surveyed, so an accurate statistic cannot be obtained. However, it can be roughly estimated based on the area affected by the disaster. The total area affected by the disaster in the province is 23,619,000 mu. Assuming that the bank of each mu of land bordering water is 1 zhang wide, and the bottom of the river is 1 zhang 5 chi wide, the total area is 35,428,500 square zhang. Excluding mountainous fields that rely entirely on natural water sources and cannot be dredged, and lightly affected areas where dredging is unnecessary, estimated to be about 50% of the total, the area of waterways that should be dredged totals 17,714,250 square zhang. Assuming an average digging depth of 2 chi, totaling 35,428,500 cubic zhang, each cubic zhang is given 2 jiao for labor and meals (usually at least 4 jiao), for a total of 7,085,700 yuan. Please allocate 12 million yuan in public bonds, which, mortgaged at a 60% discount, would yield 7.2 million yuan, which would be more than enough for work relief.

Xianju Fellow-Provincials Association Sends a Circular Telegram Begging for Relief 95

Yesterday Held a Joint Meeting of Executive and Supervisory Committees

The Xianju Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai held its first joint meeting of executive and supervisory committee members at 10:00 AM yesterday. Over 20 executive and supervisory committee members, including Wang Jingdong, attended. Representatives from the municipal party headquarters, including Zhou Lianhan, arrived to provide guidance.

Page 10

The ceremony was performed, and Chairman Wang Jingdong led all executive and supervisory committee members in swearing an oath of office. Then, Wang Jingdong, Zhu Yao, and Wang Shujin were elected as standing committee members, Zhu Yao as secretary, Wang Jingdong as general affairs, Wang Shujin as finance, Wang Wuchen, Zhang Fulun, and Zhang Songtao as investigators, Wang Huanzhong as organization, Wang Bingkun as propaganda, Xu Yingshi, Wang Yuqiu, and Zhang Chulin as social affairs, and Shou Peng, Wang Yuchen, Wang Huanlang, and Wang Yiqiu as advisors. The chairman reported on relief efforts and documents. Then, Zhou Lianze, a representative from the municipal party headquarters, provided guidance. The following resolutions were then passed: (1) Regarding the disaster of the drought in our hometown, it was resolved to issue a circular telegram begging for relief and to hold a fundraising performance. (2) The method of collecting membership fees was resolved and handed over to the finance committee for deliberation. (3) It was resolved to continue recruiting members, and the entire committee would be responsible for carrying out this task. The relief telegram reads as follows: "To all newspapers in Shanghai and to various charitable organizations: We, Xianju, have unfortunately suffered since the beginning of summer from a relentless sun and lack of rain. Wells have dried up, rivers have run dry, the earth has cracked, and the crops have withered. The disaster is the most severe in decades. Now, most of the people in the county have no rice to cook. The old and the young are helping each other, but there is no one to borrow from. Tree leaves and grass roots are used as food. They are crying out for food and cannot survive the day. The young and weak cannot survive hunger and are abandoned in ditches. The strong are taking risks and banditry is a concern. Zheng Xia's [Tang Dynasty official who submitted a map illustrating the hardships of the people], map of the suffering of the people is echoed by moaning cries everywhere and the verses of Daya Yunhan [verses from the Book of Odes about longing for rain]. This association is looking forward to our hometown with extreme pain. Every movement is related to it and we have no other responsibility. In addition to days of discussing relief measures to assist, this disaster is particularly severe, the disaster area is wide, and the mind is long and the power is cotton. What can the cup of water in a cart of firewood do for this strange disaster? Moreover, at this time of commercial depression and economic collapse, we are struggling to make ends meet. We can't use anything to help. We are asking all charitable organizations to show benevolence and provide a source of aid to rescue the disaster victims. [The] merit is immeasurable. This is the most urgent request. The Xianju Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai bows. If you are willing to donate, please send it directly to the third floor of Zhenda Silk Fabric Bureau at the intersection of Fujian Road and Fuzhou Road in Shanghai."

Macheng Disaster Relief Committee Sends Telegrams Begging for Relief to the National Government and Various Places 96

The Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai received a letter from the Macheng Disaster Relief Committee:

To all: Macheng is unfortunate to have suffered a drought disaster after a bandit disaster. Since May, there have been over 70 days without rain. Rivers and ponds have dried up, and irrigation is exhausted. The crops in districts 1, 4, 5, 6, and 7 have completely withered. In districts 2, 3, 8, and 9, one-third of the fields have not been planted, and those that have been planted have also withered. The county government has reported the disaster situation to higher levels. Now, the drought disaster is becoming more severe, rice and grain are lacking, and the people are panicking. Helpless disaster victims are applying to the county government for refugee passports. The more cunning ones are seizing large households and forcibly demanding resources. Although the county government has tried to stop this, the trend is difficult to completely eradicate. In addition, within the 9th district, dozens of people are starving to death every day. Residents by the river are mortgaging [assets] to draw water, but it is ultimately ineffective. As a result of worry and anger, there have been six suicides. The number of disaster victims inside and outside the city is increasing, with emaciated faces crying out for food. It is currently the wheat harvest, but in just two months, disaster victims will not be able to survive. The future is long, and the tragedy is unimaginable. The members of the association initially felt that the drought disaster was accidental and not an imminent crisis, but now they are so embarrassed and distressed. After silently observing the events of the past few years, they realized that the problem lies in more than one aspect. Accumulating gradually, not avoiding suspicion or resentment, they respectfully present their views with tears. Macheng has suffered a terrible bandit disaster. The 9th district and part of districts 1, 6, 7, and 8 have been bandit areas for seven years. The remaining districts have been repeatedly ravaged. Production has been reduced by more than half, and savings have been robbed completely. This is the main reason for the people's difficult lives. In addition, there are several other reasons that are sufficient to promote the collapse of the countryside. First [the looting of guest armies], since the 16th year of the Republic, guest armies, including Yuan Qian's troops, have occupied the county seat. Food and clothing are mostly provided by the local area. The losses, both public and private, are probably no less than millions of yuan. This is one reason. Second [the sharp reduction in production], the southwest countryside of our county produces cotton, and the northeast countryside produces yellow silk, wood oil, Poria cocos, and Tangfen. In recent years, the value has plummeted, less than two-thirds of the original market price. Merchants are unwilling to invest due to losses, and people are lazy to operate due to low prices. Although the autumn harvest last year was relatively ripe, farmers suffered from low grain prices and sluggish sales of local products. Financial resources were exhausted. This is two reasons. Third [the extremely heavy burden], in order to seek self-defense, the cost of the defense team was more than 200,000 yuan per year. Although the county magistrate followed the order to reduce it repeatedly, it still costs more than 11,000 yuan per month, and the temporary allocation of funds such as surtaxes, aircraft donations, and telegraph pole fees are not included in this amount. The people's strength is exhausted, and the burden is increasing day by day. This is three reasons. Fourth [the excessive number of military services], since the 2nd year of the Republic, three or four divisions of the National Army have been stationed in the county, averaging more than 3,000 long and short civilian laborers per day. For each long laborer, in addition to the price paid by the military, the people must allocate 6 to 8 yuan per month for family settlement. For each short laborer, a fee of 3 jiao must be allocated per day. Those who go have the suffering of eating in the wind and sleeping in the dew, and those who live have the worry of being exploited day by day and month by month. The abandonment of agricultural affairs is only a minor matter. This is four reasons. Fifth [the loans were not repaid], when the bandit forces were rampant in the 21st year of the Republic, the garrison had difficulty providing food. They borrowed military rice and cash from the Songbu and county town chambers of commerce, totaling more than 500,000 yuan, which has never been repaid. Other scattered invitations and donations, combined over the years, should not be less than 600,000 to 700,000 yuan. This is five reasons. Sixth [the heavy workload], in recent years, more than 200 li of the roadbed in the three sections of the Zhong Zhong Ma Tuan area in the county has been built, and 700,000 civilian laborers have been requisitioned. Farmers work from afar and provide their own food, although they are given allowances, it is not enough to cover their daily food needs, and the occupation of good fields and the filling of ponds and embankments is enough to affect the livelihood of farmers. This is six reasons. With these six reasons, merchants and civilians are in distress. Fortunately, in recent years, the harvests have been relatively bountiful and can barely be supported. Now that we are suffering from a severe drought and the autumn harvest is completely hopeless, it is like a serious illness. The vitality of the county is in despair, and it is difficult to endure. According to statistics, the total number of people in the county is 550,000, combined with the number of displaced and newly recovered, no less than 600,000. And the total amount of harvest is calculated at 5 shi per mu, but only 1,280,000 shi, an average of just over 2 shi per person per year. Therefore, in a year of good harvest, it is necessary to rely on merchant sources such as Gu Xin and Huang Deng to provide assistance. Today, the neighboring counties are also suffering from drought, and the bandits in the northwest have not been cleared. There is no place to escape to, and no funds to report to. If we do not receive condescending compassion, these hundreds of thousands of disaster victims will surely become starved corpses. Speaking of this, tears cannot be avoided. The association is complying with the request of the disaster victims to submit to the county government, and also implementing disaster relief matters in order. In terms of relief, we are investigating the actual number of remaining yi mai [types of grain], banning unscrupulous merchants from raising prices and hoarding, collecting arrears, preparing to use it to stabilize grain prices, and purchasing seeds to facilitate farmers replanting. In terms of regulation, we are requesting the resident military commander not to procure military rice locally, ordering merchants in various cities not to consume rice for profit, ordering various clan ancestral temples to move income to relieve their clansmen, persuading gentry and wealthy people to donate grain in order to stabilize market prices, and all that we can do has been actively implemented. However, the disaster area is too wide and there are too many disaster victims. It is difficult to provide relief with the strength of one county. Taking the 9th district of the county as an example, Feng and other funds have been provided to them, amounting to no less than 20,000 yuan, and more than 7,000 yuan has been allocated from the immigration funds for rations. More than 4,000 yuan was spent on buying firewood cut by refugees. The deaths are still reported monthly. Moreover, the disaster has spread throughout the county, and the number of disaster victims has increased tenfold. This is the fundamental cause of the county's vitality.

After suffering from the disasters, it is difficult to survive. I am extremely concerned about the suffering people. I respectfully request that the officials consider the suffering of the people and spread benevolent winds. The county's situation is special. I hope that they will understand and provide relief. I hope that you will not ask for thousands, leading to disaster. However, considering the current situation of the county, it is impossible to save the dying disaster victims without a major emergency relief effort. It is impossible to maintain good governance without a large number of agricultural and industrial plants. According to recent news, the provincial government has issued 5,000 yuan for agricultural relief and has handed it over to the county magistrate to purchase autumn seeds. It has also issued 17,000 yuan for work relief and has sent dozens of people from the disaster relief and preparedness association's engineering team to the county to handle it. The provincial government has spared no effort to provide relief to the county. The disaster victims in the county would not dare to ask for more than what is necessary. Only because the county is a border area, the stake is extremely high. On the one hand, it is the gateway to eastern Hubei. On the other hand, it is the screen for counties such as Gangpo. In recent years, the National Army has sacrificed countless troops and countless money to achieve considerable results. Unfortunately, they suffered from a severe drought. The bandits will surely use this opportunity to incite the disaster victims. Saving the disaster victims is a matter of life and death. It is guaranteed that they will not take risks. If food cannot be provided and order cannot be maintained, the remnant civilians will belong to both sides, and the collapse of the fence will increase the government's worries. Saving the county is to protect eastern Hubei, and protecting eastern Hubei is to protect the overall border area of the three provinces. The people of the county have survived nine deaths and one life, and have now encountered a drought disaster that has intensified. Disaster relief is difficult. The situation is urgent, so I can only tell you with tears. I earnestly request [leaders] to provide exceptional relief, allocate millions of dollars in relief funds, and save hundreds of thousands of disaster victims. This is the most urgent request. Macheng County Disaster Relief Committee, Yu Jinfang, Zheng Kangshi, Liu Rulie, and others bow.

Newly Elected Silk and Satin Industry Committee Takes Office 104

Luo Qing Elected as Chairman

And Designation of Department Heads

The Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Association held a swearing-in ceremony for newly elected and retained executive and supervisory committee members of the third term yesterday (the 6th). Representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters Zhu Ya , the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Ma Shaojin, and over twenty executive and supervisory committee members from the association attended. Luo Qing was publicly elected as chairman. The ceremony was conducted according to protocol. First, the chairman reported, and representatives from the party and chamber of commerce delivered speeches of encouragement. Then, the executive and supervisory committee members were sworn in. Subsequently, the first executive committee meeting was held, and standing committee members and the chairman were elected by ballot according to the law. Supervisors Wang Tingsong, Lu Zhengbing, Shen Qin , Lou Fengshao, Cheng Zhi , Luo Liqin, and others attended to supervise the election. Luo Qinghua, Wu Xingcuo, Zhongying, Shen Ji'en, and Pan Yisheng were elected as standing committee members, and Luo Qinghua was elected as chairman from among the standing committee members. Then, department heads were mutually recommended, with two heads for each department: Suo Zuo and Fen Li Yun for the General Affairs Department, Wang Bao and Pan Runsheng for the Economic Department, Niu Jiechen and Shao Zhang for the Organization Department, Qiu Zhihao and Xi Gongshi for the Publicity Department, and Li Wenzhi and Xu Limin for the Investigation Department. Several important cases were discussed before adjournment.

Film and Music Song Preview 107

Scheduled for the 13th at the Asia Cultural Association

In recent years, the trend of national films featuring singing, the widespread sales of radio receivers, and the abnormal development of dance halls have all contributed to society's interest and need for music and songs. Although lewd lyrics and songs catering to low-level tastes have also taken advantage of this trend, it has become a present reality that the general public has gradually developed a fondness for music through these objective influences. Currently, in China's literary, artistic, film, and music circles, there is no lack of people with aspirations to reverse the decline of popular songs in the times. In records and films, several meaningful songs are gradually being produced. After a song in the Lianhua film [Song of the Fishermen] became popular this summer, the domestic film industry has also competed to excel in this area. According to interviews conducted by reporters, the following is a compilation of songs in various new films currently being produced or about to be released by film companies: The Mingxing film [Daughter's Classic] has two songs, one is [Xiang Lei], originally written by Guo Moruo, and the other is [Afraid of Spring Returning], written by Li Pingqian. Another new film [Nostalgia] has a song [Orphanage Song], written by Ren Guang An . It is also said that there will be a song in the film [Rebirth Flower], but the title is yet to be determined. The Lianhua film [ The Road] has four songs: 1. The theme song for the road construction, named [Pioneers of the Road], written by Shi Yi; 2. A song about the theme of the road, written by Sun Yu; both of the above songs were composed by Nie Er; 3. [Swallow Song]; 4. [Fengyang Song], both are collaborative works by Ren Guang An and . Another Lianhua film, [New Woman], is said to involve mass music education and the social impact of music in its theme. Naturally, there will be new song creations in it. However, because the company strictly guards the secrets of this script, the song titles are not yet known in detail. It is said that the author is the playwright Sun Shiyi. The Tianyi Company films [Dream of the Red Chamber] and [Spring Night Song] have [Lotus Picking Song] and [Spring Night Song] written by Ren Guang An and . The Diantong Company film [Peach Tribulation] has [Graduation Song] written by Nie Er. The Yihua Company film [Immortal Fairy] has [Immortal Fairy] and [Silvery Sadness] written by Li Jinhui. Among the above songs, those that have been entrusted to Baidai Company to record include [Xiang ] sung by Hu Die, [Afraid of Spring Returning] sung by Xuan Jinglin, [Pioneers of the Road] and [The Road] sung by various stars of Jin Lianhua , [Swallow ] sung by Chen Yanyan, [Fengyang Song] sung by Li Lili, [Tea Picking Song] sung by Chen Yumei, [Graduation Song] sung by Yuan Muzhi and Chen Boer, and [Immortal Fairy] and [Silvery Sadness] sung by Bai Hong. It is said that Baidai Company will hold a preview of fifty or sixty new songs at the Asia Cultural Association on Bowuyuan Road on the 13th of this month, inviting celebrities from the local news, film, literary, artistic, drama, music, and dance circles. In addition to film songs, there will be many songs that are not easily heard elsewhere. At that time, in the sound and shadow of song, a showcase-style appreciation of new songs in our country will be a grand event in the local cultural circles.

Lu Lianfang Organizes Guanglu Paint Company 108

In recent years, China's construction industry has flourished, coupled with the eastward spread of European trends and the pursuit of modernity, the demand for paint is increasing day by day. Its use can not only increase the appearance of objects, but also has the function of preventing decay. However, although our country has established factories engaged in manufacturing, imported goods are still pouring in, making it increasingly difficult. Mr. Lu Lianfang is a person with vision. Young and handsome, he has always held the ambition of saving the country through industry. After the January 28th Incident, he founded Wanli Paint Factory and served as its general manager. For two years, he worked diligently and achieved considerable success. Business grew rapidly, but due to disagreements among shareholders, he felt it difficult to handle affairs, so he resigned from the board of directors. He gathered like-minded people to organize a new factory, named Guanglu Paint Company, found several acres of vacant land on Nan Road, designed and built the factory, and set up a preparatory office at No. 174 Huanlong Road. Soon, the latest national oil products will be sold on the market. With Mr. Lu's experience, excellent products, and business prospects, success can be predicted. The above is a recent photo of Mr. Lu.

Page 11

[Yuelaidian Sues Newspaper Vendor Cao Asan, Court Declares Him Not Guilty

Reason: Newspaper Reported the Store Sold Japanese Goods

The Defendant Has No Connection to the Matter

Yuelaidian Southern Goods Store, located at No. 356 Guangdong Road, prior to its opening this time, someone using the name "Traitor Killer" sent letters to various newspapers, stating that Yuelaidian Southern Goods Store was expanding its store and selling Japanese goods such as shark fins and squid. As a result, Guanghua Daily, Damei Evening News, Shanghai Evening News, etc., all published the news. During Yuelaidian's opening, newspaper vendors brought the above newspapers to the store entrance and shouted to sell them. Yuelaidian's manager reported to the police station, and on September 29th at 8:00 PM, the police arrested Cao Asan, a newspaper vendor from Tongzhou. The next morning, he was sent to the First Special District Local Court, requesting punishment in accordance with Article 35, Item 12 of the Regulations on Punishment for Violation of Police Regulations. After interrogation by Judge Shen, the case was adjourned for further investigation, and the defendant was detained. The day before yesterday, Judge Shen again ordered Cao Asan to be brought before the court. After questioning, the court held that the newspaper's content was the responsibility of the newspaper itself and that the defendant had no connection to the matter. Cao Asan was acquitted and released in court.

National Radio Stations Scheduled to Change Names 112

Effective December 1st

The Ministry of Communications, in view of the fact that the names of many cities and provinces where telegraph bureaus and radio stations are located have been changed, and that the names of the bureaus and stations still largely use the old names, which are inconsistent with the local names and easily lead to misunderstandings, should be corrected separately to ensure uniformity. It is understood that the ministry yesterday ordered the renamed bureaus and stations to implement the changes from December 1st of this year. Within the first three months, when receiving telegrams sent by the bureaus and stations, in addition to translating and noting the name of the sending bureau and station, the receiving bureau and station should also add the old name to benefit the public.

Pilgrimage Train and Freight Train Collide 113

Two Freight Cars Derailed

Pilgrimage Train Continues as Usual

Yesterday, the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway had a special train due to the pilgrimage to the Chang'an Catholic Church. Over three hundred Chinese and foreign ladies and gentlemen of faith attended to participate in the Mass, so the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway specially opened the No. 901 train, equipped with four third-class passenger cars, one second/third-class passenger car, and one official car. It departed from the South Station yesterday morning at 6:05 AM. Unexpectedly, when the train reached Laolonghua Station (at 6:18 AM), the Hangzhou-bound No. 804 night freight train also arrived at that time, so it stopped to wait for the interchange. The freight train had to give way to the main line, but before it had completely entered the siding, the special train started to depart, colliding with the No. 5619 and No. 10143 freight cars at the rear of the freight train, damaging four sections of the siding track. The two freight cars also derailed, but fortunately the impact was light and they did not overturn. The main line track from Shanghai to Hangzhou was not damaged, so the special train stopped for about ten minutes and then proceeded to Chang'an Station. The Laolonghua Station Master immediately telegraphed the South Station to report the accident. Zhong Wenjiang, the head of the train operations section stationed at the South Station, immediately notified the engineering department and dispatched over a hundred craftsmen from the locomotive department's Longtou depot on a salvage vehicle, supervised by Director Zhong. At 7:00 AM, they rode to Laolonghua, first repairing the four damaged sections of track and then using a crane to lift the two derailed freight cars back onto the track. The traffic was restored to normal after about 2:00 PM.

Public Utilities Bureau Bus Causes Accident 114

Collides with China General Omnibus Yesterday

Traffic Suspended for Over Forty Minutes

Yesterday morning at 9:25 AM, China General Omnibus Company's Route 3 trolleybus No. 45, driven by driver , was traveling from Xiaodongmen to Laoximen Circular Road. When approaching the trolleybus stop in front of the Laoda Fang candy store in Laoximen from north to south, a Public Utilities Bureau bus No. 10008, driven by driver Wang Jinsheng, also traveling from north to south, tried to overtake the trolleybus on the right and reach the stop first, resulting in a collision. The trolleybus's protective iron plate and crossbar were damaged, and the bus's wheel hub and fender were also damaged. The drivers called the police to the scene. The China General Omnibus Company invited the Huafang Photo Studio to photograph the accident scene for negotiation purposes. The police from the Wenmiao Police Station brought both parties to the Wenmiao Road Police Station for investigation. Trolleybus traffic was suspended for over forty minutes.

Chen's Couple Leaves Behind a Daughter
