Chen Fangruo, a native of Hubei, about 37 or 38 years old, lived in Shanghai as a writer. Witness Sees Three Punches

Both Suspects Deny Accusations

Gao Huailin, a native of Yangzhou, was also an apprentice at the same factory. On August 31st of this year, while working at the factory, Gao asked Jiang to add coal, but Jiang refused, leading to an argument and a physical altercation. Another apprentice, Zhou Dayun, saw this and stepped forward to mediate. However, Jiang Xiaoerzi not only refused to listen but also used foul language. Zhou, enraged, rushed forward and punched Jiang violently. Jiang Xiaoerzi collapsed to the ground, barely breathing. The factory manager heard about this and ordered a car to take him to the Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road. He died in the hospital on September 3rd. The police arrested Zhou Dayun and Gao Huailin and sent them to the former Sixth District Police Station and then to the local court. Prosecutor Wu Deying conducted a preliminary hearing and brought charges against them in the criminal court. The trial was held yesterday morning by Judge Zhang Shao in the Fifth Court. The factory manager testified that according to another worker, Gao Huailin asked Jiang Xiaoerzi to add coal, but Jiang refused, leading to an argument and a physical altercation. Zhou Dayun stepped forward to mediate, but he did not witness the fight. Jiao Yitang's Opinion on the Aconite Tide 117

National Medicine and National Drugs Should Unite to Resist Foreign Aggression

Since the Ningbo County Aconite Shell Cooperative raised the price of high-quality aconite shells, triggering a trend in the Shanghai national medical community to not use aconite shells, and with the cooperative and Shanghai medical and pharmaceutical organizations holding conflicting views that are difficult to reconcile, the New Voice News reporter, in order to clarify the truth, made a special trip to Beijing to visit Jiao Yitang, a Central Committee member and director of the Central National Medical Hall, to inquire about his opinion. Jiao expressed deep emotion. Furthermore, Wu Qianqian, a local national doctor, also expressed fair opinions on the aconite shell trend. The details are recorded below:

Jiao Yitang's Speech: Jiao first stated that he has never had prejudice against the national medicine and pharmaceutical community. However, national medicine and national drugs are currently in a turbulent situation, and they are too busy uniting to resist foreign aggression to have any intention of capitalizing on scarcity and inciting internal strife, which would be a misguided strategy. From the cooperative's perspective, raising prices would only help foreign goods to be sold at dumping prices and exploit the hard work of farmers and workers, effectively shortening the lifespan of our national medicine and drugs. He only hopes that they will consider the welfare of patients and repent. Just like the [Minsheng] and [Foci] pharmaceutical factories in Shanghai, which use Chinese raw materials, extract and test ingredients, improve processing methods, and resist foreign goods, saving considerable losses to the country, which is beneficial to both national economy and the people's livelihood, why must they profit by sucking the fat of their own country's sick and laugh at foreign countries? He believes that the Shanghai medical and pharmaceutical organizations and the cooperative have many enlightened people, and that with the public opinion community upholding justice, both parties will be able to consider the overall situation. The cooperative should still sincerely and strictly implement the contract signed with the National Pharmaceutical Association to be effective, so that drug prices will fall, the aconite tide can be avoided from expanding, and the well-being of patients will be taken as the premise. In the twelfth issue of the Guanghua Medical and Pharmaceutical Magazine, Jiao's detailed opinions on the aconite shell trend are published.

Wu Qianqian's Opinion: Furthermore, Wu Qianqian, a local national doctor, expressed his opinions on the aconite shell trend from three perspectives related to the Department of Agriculture and Politics as follows: (1) The issue of rural areas: Patients use medicine at a certain time, while the livelihood of farmers is related to the countryside. Some argue that the rural economy is currently bankrupt, and it is not possible to destroy the rural economy by boycotting aconite shells. They are unaware that the medical community's refusal to use aconite shells is to resist the cooperative's existing goods and to hope that farmers will sell as much aconite shell as possible. If the supply of aconite shell already exceeds demand, then there is no reason for this. Selling aconite shell is prevalent throughout China, but its production is only limited to a part of Zhejiang Province. If the price is low, it will harm the farmers of Zhejiang, which is not a fact. (2) The issue of provincial administration: Zhejiang Province approved the cooperative's exclusive operating rights. Its initial intention was nothing more than to benefit Zhejiang in Zhejiang, but it did not consider that the price would rise to such an extent. The benefit to the people of Zhejiang has not been seen, but the impact on the patients and medical and pharmaceutical communities nationwide is enormous. If its malpractices take effect, then Rehmannia glutinosa will be hoarded in Henan, Coptis chinensis will be hoarded in Sichuan, Aucklandia lappa will be hoarded in Guangdong, and Codonopsis pilosula will be hoarded in Shanxi. All medicines will skyrocket, and in severe cases, they will disappear from the market. The future of national medicine is unimaginable. This humble person from Zhejiang also does not want to hear about the selfishness and self-interest of the people of Zhejiang. Therefore, not promoting local methods must be included in the ban, and promoting local methods as much as possible will make the price fair and the trend will cease. (3) The issue of substitutes: Peucedanum praeruptorum and aconite shell have similar properties and effects. Using them as substitutes does not affect the overall situation. However, a few Chinese medicine practitioners believe that they cannot be substituted, and some patients even point out their disadvantages. Some Western doctors even consider Peucedanum praeruptorum to be a digestive medicine and aconite shell to be a respiratory medicine. This is due to stubborn prejudice on the one hand, ignorance on the other, and Western doctors' lack of knowledge of Chinese medicine, none of which are accurate arguments. Peucedanum praeruptorum and aconite shell are not comparable to life-saving drugs. If their effects are similar, how can substitution cause illness? In the past, when there was no aconite shell, only Fritillaria cirrhosa, it was never heard that coughs and phlegm were difficult to treat without aconite shell. Furthermore, Zhu Huilao said that he once coughed up blood due to substituting Peucedanum praeruptorum for aconite shell, which is absolutely not the case in pharmacology or medicine. If substituting Pinellia ternata for aconite shell could cause coughing up blood, it is possible. Peucedanum praeruptorum eliminates phlegm and lowers qi, and is even used in prescriptions for coughing up blood. How can it cause hemoptysis? Even if it does, it is likely a coincidence. Furthermore, both Peucedanum praeruptorum and aconite shell are respiratory medicines. Considering them to be digestive medicines is a mistake. However, this humble person hopes that temporary substitution is acceptable, but long-term substitution will ultimately be inconvenient. It is only hoped that the cooperative will broaden its horizons and sincerely cooperate with the medical and pharmaceutical community, so that drug prices will be slightly lower, and patients will benefit more. Because I heard the sound of arguing, I rushed forward and saw Zhou Dayun punching Jiang Xiao Erzi in the back three times. The interrogating official ordered the detention of Zhou Dayun and Gao Huailin to be brought to the case. Zhou Dayun confessed that he was seventeen years old, from Suqian, and lived in Minghua Lane, Robert Road. (Question) Jiang Afu said that you punched Jiang Xiao Erzi three times, is that true? (Answer) I went forward to pull him away and did not hit him. I was really wronged. Gao Huailin confessed that he was eleven years old and lived in Yufu Lane, Meiyuan Intersection, Gonghe Road. (Question) Why did you argue with Jiang Xiao Erzi? (Answer) The stove fire was about to go out, so I called Jiang Xiao Erzi to add coal. Jiang refused and scolded me instead. (Question) Did you hit him? (Answer) I did not hit him, but I grabbed and twisted him. Zhou Dayun came to pull him away. According to the statement of the deceased's brother, Jiang Ade, my brother was brutally beaten to death by Zhou Dayun's punches. I request that justice be served. At this point in the interrogation, the interrogating official invited prosecutor Wu Deying to the court. After the arguments were presented, the debate began. The lawyer Liu Xiang, hired by the two defendants, rose to defend them for a long time, requesting a verdict of innocence. The judge believed that the conclusion had been reached and scheduled the sentencing for 9:00 a.m. on the 8th of this month. The two defendants were remanded in custody.

Siblings Fighting Over Property 118

Under the law, self-prosecution is not allowed.

The statute of limitations has also expired.

| Jiang Jingwan's Lawsuit Dismissed |

Jiang Jingwan, a Nanjing woman residing at No. 47, South Gaoshou Lane, Haining Road, is 38 years old. She recently hired a lawyer to file a criminal self-prosecution with the First Special Court against her younger brother, Jiang Guoying (37 years old, residing at No. 58, Lane 41, Carter Road), for violating Articles 356 of the Criminal Law by encroaching on their deceased father's estate. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng presided over the interrogation in the Fifth Criminal Court. The defendant also appeared with a lawyer. The plaintiff, Jiang Jingwan, stated that her biological father was Jiang Xingqi, and her adoptive father was Jiang Shengshu. Her adoptive father passed away when she was sixteen years old. Because she was away in another city, she did not know how the property rights were handled. It was not until October of the year before last that she learned that the estate had been divided. In April of last year, she entrusted her aunt to consult with the defendant, but the defendant refused to hand over her share of the property and thực hiện encroachment, hence the lawsuit. After Judge Huang briefly questioned the defendant, he ruled that since the plaintiff and defendant were siblings, self-prosecution was not allowed under the law, and the statute of limitations had also expired. Therefore, the self-prosecution was dismissed, and she was advised to file a lawsuit in the Civil Court.

Citizens of Pudong Request the Construction of a Pudong Water Plant 120

High Population Density Makes Water Collection Difficult

Hygiene and Fire Prevention Are Even More Important

According to Xin Sheng News, the Municipal Government once planned to build a water plant in Pudong, but it was shelved due to lack of funds. The citizens of Pudong feel quite inconvenienced. In recent years, the population density in Pudong has increased, and the drinking water for citizens is dirty, and water collection is difficult. In the event of a fire, it is often difficult to contain the spread due to the distance of the water source. Both hygiene and fire prevention are even more important. The local citizens believe that the establishment of a water plant in Pudong only requires 230,000 yuan, but the Municipal Government shelved it on the grounds of lack of funds, while a construction project that is not urgently needed in Puxi, costing hundreds of thousands of yuan, is immediately started. Furthermore, the tax burden of the citizens of Pudong is no different from that of the citizens of Puxi. Why is the enjoyment of material things so unfair? It is now heard that 61 businesses, including Chen Tai, Dongsheng, Xiangtai, Zhang Tianyi, Lao Songsheng, Shunxing, Rentai, Xintai, Qiandefeng, Xinxingchang, Yongyuantai, Dingshengtai, Gongtai, Yichun, Bin Da, Datonghe, and Wanyuan, have jointly submitted a petition to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, requesting that it be forwarded to the Municipal Government for review and approval, and that the two bureaus of finance and public works be instructed to complete the Pudong water plant as soon as possible to benefit the people's livelihood.

The Machine Union's Travel Group Is Scheduled to Go to Suzhou for On-Site Inspection 121

According to Xin Sheng News, the Machine-Made National Goods Factory Union of this city is striving to promote and introduce national goods in order to develop the country's industry. The travel inspection group organized by the union is scheduled to go to Suzhou for inspection. The details are as follows:

Travel Guidelines: The guidelines for the travel inspection group are: (1) The purpose of this group is to investigate industries in various places, inspect local customs and cultures, appreciate local scenery, connect members' feelings, in order to seek business development and physical health. (2) All member factories of this union are eligible to be members of this group. (3) The number of members in this group is limited to 50 people. (4) The group will hold one activity every day when traveling outside. (5) The travel locations and return dates of this group will be temporarily notified after a meeting of the standing committee. (6) Each member participating in the trip must prepay various travel expenses, the amount of which will be temporarily determined (surplus will be returned, deficiency will be supplemented, other miscellaneous expenses will be borne by the member). (7) Anyone participating in the trip must notify the union three days in advance for registration. (8) Anyone who has registered and paid but is unable to participate due to unforeseen circumstances may ask someone to represent them. If no one is asked to substitute, the fees paid will not be refunded. (9) All participants must comply with the time and meeting place specified in the previous notice. (10) If members wish to propose a travel location and request the group to travel there, it must be signed by more than five people before it can be processed. (11) Several union staff members will be responsible for hospitality during the trip. (12) These guidelines are subject to change at any time if they are not perfect.

Going to Suzhou for Inspection: Yesterday, the union notified its members, saying: "Greetings. After reviewing the travel inspection group guidelines drafted by the administration department, which were passed at the 27th meeting of the Standing Committee of the last session on April 3rd of this year, Song Wei Peidao was publicly elected as the head of the travel inspection group at the 4th meeting of the Executive Committee of this session. At this time when sweet osmanthus is fragrant and the autumn breeze is refreshing, it is a good time to inspect travel businesses, both physically and mentally. Suzhou is a place where talented people gather, and it is also a place of beautiful mountains and rivers. Taihu Lake is vast and floating, and the 72 peaks are spiritually deep and secluded. One can admire the ancient sites of the King of Wu. Moreover, national goods factories in the area are booming. Visiting them will provide a reference. It is scheduled to depart on the 14th of this month (Sunday) at 8:00 a.m. by special express train and return to Shanghai by special express train at 9:46 p.m. on the same day. The travel expense is 10 yuan per person (surplus will be returned, deficiency will be supplemented). If your esteemed factory sends personnel to participate (and family members are welcome), please gather in the North Station hall before 7:30 a.m. on the day for the trip. The attached regulations and reply slips should be filled out and sent to the union for registration and payment."

Anqin Grand Master to Depart Tomorrow 127

Boarding the Italian Liner Conte Verde for Hong Kong

Grand Master Anqin Hutuktu, since arriving in Shanghai on the 3rd to wait for the ship to return to Tibet, has stayed in Shanghai and resided in the Buddhist Pure Land Society on Hart Road. At the invitation of the society and the two Buddhist associations of China and Shanghai, he lectured for four days. Since the opening of the altar on the 5th, many people have been listening to the Grand Master's lectures every day. Today is the last day. The first three days were lectures on the Diamond Sutra, and women and children were prohibited from listening. Today is a lecture on the Guanyin Sutra, and women and children are welcome to listen. As for the Grand Master's departure from Shanghai, it has been decided that he will set off tomorrow on the Italian mail ship Conte Verde. All of his more than 100 pieces of luggage have been handed over to the China Travel Service for transportation to Hong Kong. The Grand Master and his party of more than 40 people are scheduled to board the ship tomorrow. Party and government agencies in this city and various Buddhist charitable organizations will send representatives to the Jianggan wharf to see them off.

Xu Shiying and Others Sent Letters to Leaders of All Sectors to Participate in the Charity Relief Association 128

Establishment Meeting to Be Held at the Chamber of Commerce on the 14th

So That People in Dire Straits Can Be Rescued Sooner

Xu Shiying, chairman of the National Government Relief Commission, discussed relief measures with local celebrities due to the severe drought this year. It was decided to formally establish the All Sectors Fundraising Charity Relief Association in Shanghai on the 14th of this month. Details have been recorded in yesterday's newspaper. It is learned that Xu et al. sent letters to all charitable organizations, leaders of all sectors, and local celebrities today, requesting them to participate at that time. The original letter said: "Greetings. Since the beginning of summer this year, rainfall has been untimely, and severe drought has occurred. Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan, Su Yu, Hebei, Jin, Gansu, Qian and other provinces have suffered from 133.83 million mu of damaged farmland, with more than 10 million people affected. After years of disasters, they have suffered this great calamity again. In the blink of an eye, the winter season is approaching, and hunger and cold are intertwined. The impact is unbearable. As long as we have a breath, relief cannot be delayed. We are launching a charity relief association to raise funds for relief. It has been decided to hold a founding meeting and inaugural meeting at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce at 4:00 p.m. on the 14th of this month. We have long admired your compassion and enthusiasm for good deeds. We earnestly request you to take time to attend, and jointly devise relief strategies so that people in dire straits can be rescued sooner. The merit is immeasurable."

Tongrenhe Paint Shop Sued by German Company for Counterfeiting 129

Tongrenhe Paint Shop, located at No. 80, Minguo Road, French Concession, is owned by Xu Chengdong (35 years old this year) from Shaoxing Yuyao. It has been in business for many years. It is now being sued by Li Anha (transliteration), the English manager of the German Defu Foreign Firm at No. 261 Sichuan Road, who has found that the shop is counterfeiting the Candle Trademark paint sold by the firm, which has affected the firm's business. According to intelligence reports, the French police were asked to investigate. The head of the police approved the request and ordered Chinese and Western detectives to search the premises. 3,500 sheets of Candle Trademark paper were seized, along with the shop owner Xu Chengdong, and taken to the police station. Xu confessed that in 1929, he ordered five large barrels of Candle paint from Defu Foreign Firm for the purpose of making candles. Later, with the consent of the firm, he repackaged the barreled paint into small tin cans for sale and commissioned the Xinmin Printing House in Xinxin Lane in the Chinese area to print 5,000 sheets of Candle Trademark paper for distribution and sale. 1,400 cans have been sold, but due to the inferior quality of the goods, customers often returned them. The seized Trademark paper is what was left over from before. According to the confession, the head of the police ordered Xu to leave and await further investigation. The police station transferred the case to the Second Special Court a few days ago. The police station lawyer filed a public prosecution in accordance with Article 269 of the Criminal Law for obstructing agricultural, industrial, and commercial crime. Judge Wu Fanglian heard the case in the Eighth Criminal Court. Since the defendant Xu Chengdong was not present, the police station lawyer and the plaintiff stated the case. The court ordered that the defendant be summoned to court on the 13th for further questioning.

Old Man Run Over by Car 130

At around 3:30 p.m. yesterday, at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Chengdu Road, an old man over sixty years old, wearing a gray serge jacket and a black straight-weave mandarin jacket and with a long beard, was crossing Jing'an Temple Road from the Chengdu Road intersection. Unexpectedly, at that time, a public concession Second Road tram was speeding by. Unable to avoid it, the tram knocked the old man down, sending him flying several feet away. He suffered injuries to his head and chest, among other places, and immediately lost consciousness. Fortunately, a nearby policeman noticed the incident and quickly summoned an ambulance to rush him to the hospital for treatment. However, due to the severity of his injuries and his advanced age, he died despite medical attention. The hospital reported the death to the police station, which transferred the body to the coroner's office for examination this morning. An investigation into the deceased's family is underway.

Young Man Commits Suicide by Taking Poison in Huitong Hotel 131

At around 6:00 p.m. the night before last, a young male traveler came to Huitong Hotel at No. 13, Yude Lane, Yunnan Road, Public Concession. He claimed to be named Lu Qian, 21 years old, a local, and a businessman. The bellboy led him to room 33, with a daily rate of 70 cents per dollar. He paid one dollar. After the bellboy brought tea and water, he closed the door and went to bed. At midnight, he secretly swallowed a large amount of tranquilizing water in an attempt to commit suicide. Fortunately, the hotel bellboy discovered it early and immediately reported it to the Lao Zha Police Station, which dispatched Chinese policeman No. 105 to the scene and summoned ambulance No. 83 to transport him to Renji Hospital for treatment. Two suicide notes were found on the young man, one to his elder brother and one to his mother, stating that he wanted to get married but was overwhelmed by financial pressure and wished to escape the mortal world as soon as possible to end his life. Due to taking too much poison, his life is still in critical condition. The police station is currently contacting the young man's family.

Room 221 of the Da Zhong Hotel

Claiming to Be Liu Zhijing from Hubei Province

The Xujiahui Observatory issued the following weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: Sunny around Shandong, wind from southeast to southwest. Middle reaches of the Yangtze River, cloudy and cool, with northeast to east wind. Lower reaches of the Yangtze River, northeast to southeast wind. East Sea to Taiwan Strait, cloudy, turning overcast, northeast wind very strong. The typhoon west of the Xisha Islands continues to move westward. The typhoon southwest of the Ogasawara Islands will move northward. The center of the first typhoon reached within 120 miles of 22 degrees north latitude and 125 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM, moving northward, wind force unknown. The center of the second typhoon reached within 60 miles of 18 degrees 30 north latitude and 140 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM, moving westward, wind force fierce. Letters to the Editor 145

To the esteemed editor of Shen Bao:

I am writing in response to the news item in your newspaper on the 7th of this month regarding the collapse of our factory's drying platform, which injured people. The information in your report is not consistent with the facts. Our factory's drying platform is made of wood. At the time of the incident yesterday, work had already stopped, and the workers were resting on the platform. Unfortunately, it suddenly collapsed, causing minor injuries. They have been treated at the hospital and have recovered. The report in your newspaper that the incident occurred while they were tanning leather and that they were seriously injured by being crushed under a pile of tiles, with some suffering life-threatening injuries to the abdomen, is based on hearsay. We are concerned that the public may not understand the truth, so we are writing to request that your newspaper make a correction.

Sincerely,

Jin Xie Ji Leather Factory

7th

To the esteemed editor of Shen Bao:

I have read the news item in your "Local News" column on September 28th, titled "Zhou Guansan Sued by His Wife." It states that Zhou Guansan's younger brother, Zhou Lansheng, sent a letter to his brother containing various slanderous remarks. I was shocked and dismayed upon reading this. Zhou Guansan's family has lived in Hushen, Hangzhou for generations and is known for their virtuous and upright character. They have always valued propriety and righteousness. His ancestors and father were respected members of the community. Zhou Guansan has followed in their footsteps, carefully maintaining his self-respect in all his actions. He is a handsome and promising young man, highly regarded in his hometown. We suspect that malicious individuals are attempting to damage his reputation by fabricating facts and spreading rumors to confuse the public. We, as long-time residents of Hushen, have a better understanding of the situation. We know Zhou Guansan's behavior from childhood to adulthood and are fully aware of the truth. How can the unsubstantiated claims of his younger brother Lansheng, based solely on hearsay, be used as the sole tool to damage Zhou Guansan's reputation? Although this matter is not our concern, we feel compelled to speak out because the facts are clear, and truth must be distinguished from falsehood. We have long admired your newspaper for upholding justice, so we are writing to request a correction to prevent confusion and ensure accuracy. We would be grateful if you would grant our request.

Sincerely,

Zhao Shunnian, Wang Huting, Fang Zirong, Shen Shuyi, Wu Dasheng, Jin Jiayun, Ma Yumen, Xie Songsheng, residents of Hushen, Hangzhou

To the esteemed editor of Shen Bao:

I am writing on behalf of my client, Mr. Hong Rummei of Wah Sin Hong Kee Company, who informed me that on the afternoon of the 5th of this month, I went to the Xin Sheng Hospital to pay a fee, but the hospital was suddenly raided by the police, which implicated me as well. After being taken to the police station, I explained the situation and provided proof, and I was immediately released. However, the news item in your newspaper on the 6th, regarding the morphine seized at Xin Sheng Hospital, mistakenly identified me as a mixing engineer and failed to mention that I was released on the spot and not sent to court. I believe this is a misrepresentation of the facts and is based on hearsay. I am writing to request a correction to ensure accuracy.

Sincerely,

Lawyer Yan Zhi

Received October 7th

Regarding the "Wang Guoliang, Young Man, Affair with Old Woman" news item:

We are writing in response to a report in your newspaper (dated the 4th) that Mr. Yu's husband, Wang Guoliang, the owner of Shun Chang Xiang Foreign Goods Store at No. 990, Betang Road, Xujiahui, had an affair with an old woman and that Mr. Yu caught them in the act. This is inconsistent with the facts. We would like to present the following key points for correction:

(1) Yu, Guoliang's wife, is surnamed Tong, not Xu as reported in the newspaper.

(2) The old woman, Zhu Liu, is a relative of Yu's family, and the two families had a close relationship. Later, due to a dispute over money, they became resentful of Yu. This spring, they even had a verbal altercation. Unexpectedly, after the altercation, she directly told Yu's husband, which caused discord in the family because Yu's husband only heard one side of the story. This escalated into physical and verbal abuse from all three sides. Due to the unresolved dispute, they went to the French Concession police station to request mediation and sign a settlement agreement. The old woman voluntarily agreed to stay away from Xujiahui. Therefore, the report that Yu gathered a group of women and caught the old woman and the young man in the act and took them to the Second Special Court is completely unfounded.

(3) After the settlement at the police station, Yu's husband continued to work at the store every day, as witnessed by relatives and customers. The statement that he moved to West Xinqiao to live secretly with the old woman is also absurd.

(4) Yu's husband has not been ill recently, let alone bedridden, which has been witnessed by many people. Therefore, the report of his being bedridden is absolutely incorrect.

(5) On the 3rd of this month, the old woman Zhu Liu, her anger reignited, violated her previous agreement, and returned to Xujiahui. She stood at the tram stop in front of Yu's store, staring into the store. Suddenly, she got off the tram and attempted to cause trouble. Yu was forced to take her to the Catholic Church for judgment. The matter was resolved after mediation.

The key points of the actual events, which differ significantly from your newspaper's report, are as stated above. We respectfully request that you make a prompt correction.

Sincerely,

Wang Tong (personally signed)

Reading News, Issue 30 147

Compiled by the Reading Guidance Department of the Shen Bao Circulation Library

Table of Contents

(1) Announcement of the Suspension of "Reading Q&A"

(2) Special Feature

I. News of Reading Life

II. News of the YMCA Reading Club

Announcement of the Suspension of "Reading Q&A"

Time flies so quickly. "Reading Q&A" has met with you for a full nine months. Apart from the Lunar New Year holidays and occasional suspensions due to insufficient space in the newspaper, which occurred no more than ten times, tens of thousands of readers have been reading it every day. We are very honored to have gained so many supporters in spirit, but on the other hand, we cannot help but feel ashamed.

What have we actually given to the readers? On the eve of this suspension, we did some serious reflection. Before we part ways, we must make a confession: we cannot deny that what we have given to others, if not zero, is too limited.

This is by no means a humble statement. First, because "Reading Q&A" is only part of the work of this department, and this department itself is only a department of the library, we do not have enough time to make "Reading Q&A" more vibrant and practical. Second, because of the space constraints of the newspaper, news articles are often squeezed together, and the "Reading Q&A" often has to be cut into sections, making it difficult for readers to connect the beginning and the end, making reading it equivalent to not reading it. Third, because the people who write the reading Q&As are mostly bookworms, who are too far removed from the actual lives of shop assistants and apprentices, the things they write inevitably carry a scholarly atmosphere and cannot be approached by people who truly lack education. Fourth, we have also received many well-intentioned criticisms and rigorous corrections from various quarters. We have tried hard to be impartial, but our efforts have been in vain, and we cannot live up to everyone's expectations. In short, after reflecting on ourselves, we only feel ashamed and blame ourselves. Now we do not want to continue doing this work that we cannot do well. We would like to thank and apologize to all those who care about us.

What about the future? We are library workers, and our work in reading guidance in the library will not end because of this. On the contrary, we can concentrate our efforts on other aspects. At the same time, we can add a note to console readers: Reading Life will soon publish a reading magazine called Reading Life Biweekly. In the future, any questions about reading may be discussed in that publication. Now that we are temporarily suspending this corner of the newspaper, you will probably not feel too lonely!

Before and after this, we sincerely hope that readers will continue to acquire new knowledge in their daily lives. Today's China is in a very rich era. As long as you are true to your life and diligent in acquiring knowledge, you can gain knowledge everywhere. We encourage you to read, but at the same time, do not trust books too much. We encourage you to spend a minute on the street or in the market, rather than returning to a clean and bright study. We wish you all the best.

Special Feature 148

I. News from "Reading Life"

I. Reading Life will be edited by the Reading Life Society and published by the Shanghai Magazine Company.

Reading Life was originally planned to be edited by the Reading Guidance Department of the Shen Bao Circulation Library. However, due to insufficient manpower in that department, it will now be edited by the Reading Life Society. The president of the society is still Mr. Li Gongpu. People from Shanghai's cultural circles with experience in teaching have been invited to form the Reading Life Society. Reading Life will be published biweekly, with approximately 50,000 words per issue, and will be published by the Shanghai Magazine Company. The first issue will be published next month.

II. Solicitation of Contributions for "Reading Life"

The content of "Reading Life" has been announced in Issue 27 of this publication and will remain largely unchanged. The publication pays special attention to the investigation of readers' lives in various social classes, so it particularly requests contributions of "Life Records" from shop assistants, apprentices, workers, soldiers, farmers, and all other professionals, even those who do not usually write articles. All readers who can write, regardless of whether their writing is good or not, are welcome to submit their unique life experiences to the publication. Those who cannot write but would like to share their lives can write to the publication, and reporters will be sent to record their stories. However, these life records should not contain any idle talk, and each article should not exceed 3,000 words. At the same time, we also welcome "Self-Study Experience Talks" and "Reading Notes" from people with busy lives, but each article should be limited to 1,500 words. Please send your contributions to Reading Life Society, Shanghai Magazine Company, No. 30, Sima Road, Shanghai.

II. News of the YMCA Reading Club

The YMCA Reading Club held its second inaugural meeting at the Eight Immortals Bridge on the 7th of this month. More than 150 members attended, and Mr. Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, personally attended to provide guidance. The meeting began at 9:00 AM as scheduled, with Mr. Li Gongpu presiding. Director Pan gave a speech, which mainly covered the purpose of reading, the purpose of the YMCA in running the reading club, the attitude towards reading, and the outlook on life, among other things. His arguments were brilliant. The full text of his speech will be published in the YMCA publication. Representatives from the advanced class, Yang Lijun, and the elementary class, Wang Wenqing, also gave speeches. After the speeches, the classes were divided. There are two classes: advanced and elementary. The meeting time is still set for Thursdays from 7:30 PM to 9:30 PM and Sundays from 9:30 AM to 11:30 AM at the YMCA at Eight Immortals Bridge. It is reported that there are still many vacancies for members in the club. People who are interested in reading are welcome to join. For application procedures, please write to the YMCA at Eight Immortals Bridge.

Hua Bei Games Stadium to be Inaugurated on National Day 150

Athletes from All Regions Continue to Arrive in Tianjin

Preparations Nearing Completion

(Special Dispatch from Tianjin, 7th) The stadium for the Hua Bei Games was completed last night. The inauguration ceremony will be held on the morning of National Day. The Shanxi athletes arrived yesterday afternoon, and the Qingdao team is on its way. The preparations for the opening of the Games on National Day are complete.

Inauguration Ceremony of the Games Stadium 151

Tianjin, 7th (Special Dispatch) The Hua Bei Games will hold the inauguration ceremony of the Hebei Province Sports Stadium at 8:00 AM on the 10th. The order of events is as follows: (1) Opening ceremony, (2) Officials and athletes enter the stadium, (3) All stand at attention, (4) Sing the party song, (5) Give the highest salute to the party flag and the portrait of the Prime Minister, (6) The chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will, (7) Silent tribute, (8) Chairman's speech, (5) Guest speeches, (10) Inauguration ceremony, A: Chairman's report, B: Release of doves, C: Setting off firecrackers, (10)(1) Ceremony concludes.

Opening Ceremony and Athletes' Oath 152

Regulations for the October 10th Opening Ceremony of the North China Games: (1) Opening Music; (2) All Rise; (3) Flag Raising and 18 Gun Salute; (4) Chairman's Opening Remarks; (5) Preparatory Committee's Report on Preparations; (6) All Athletes Take Oath; (7) President and Vice-President's Admonitory Speech; (8) Speeches by Leaders of Participating Delegations; (9) Chief Referee's Admonitory Speech; (10) Speech by Representative of the North China Sports Federation; (11) Photography; (12) Assembly Staff and Athletes Leave the Field Led by the Band; (13) Ceremony Concludes. The Athletes' Oath, as decided by the organizing committee, is as follows: "I solemnly pledge to uphold the spirit of physical education promoted by our Party's founder, to participate in the competition as an amateur athlete, to strictly abide by all the rules of the Games, and to obey the referees' decisions. I solemnly swear." Order of Units in Formation: Military Band, Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Harbin, Qingdao, Shaanxi, Suiyuan, Chahar, Shanxi, Henan, Shandong, Pingjin (Beiping and Tianjin), Hebei.

Shanxi Delegation Arrives in Tianjin Yesterday Afternoon 153

The Shanxi delegation arrived in Tianjin this afternoon at 4:30 PM, consisting of 91 officials, male and female athletes. This includes 20 male senior track and field athletes, 8 basketball players, 15 soccer players, 12 volleyball players, 4 tennis players, 6 for national martial arts, 8 male intermediate basketball players, 4 track and field athletes, 4 tennis players, 1 female track and field athlete. The Wang Chun and Chunyuan sisters are also coming. Female track and field athlete Qi Tao is 17 years old, a second-year student at Jin Pingmin Middle School, and will participate in the 100-meter, 50-meter, and long jump events. In the Shanxi preliminaries, her results were 14.8 seconds for 100 meters, 7.8 seconds for 50 meters, and 4.25 meters for the long jump. Her usual times are 14.2 seconds for 100 meters, 7.2 seconds for 50 meters, and 4.32 meters for the long jump. Shanxi's sprint king Wang Shuqing's time is 11.3 seconds. Chen Dengying's 1500-meter time is 4 minutes and 25 seconds. Gu Desheng, Chen Dengying, and Wang Huibin's 10,000-meter times all broke 35 minutes, with Gu Desheng's time of 34 minutes and 37 seconds being the best. Shandong athlete Niu Hongquan's 10,000-meter time is 34 minutes and 55 seconds, suggesting future competition in the 10,000 meters will be between Shanxi and Shandong. Chen Shusen, the former Far Eastern Games 10,000-meter representative, has also arrived, but may not compete due to lack of recent training.

Chu Minyi Arrives in Tianjin Yesterday 154

Chu Minyi arrived in Tianjin at 4:20 AM this morning. Hebei Provincial Committee members and Games officials welcomed him at the station. After disembarking, he went to the Provincial Government Club for refreshments, and then to the Huizhong Hotel to rest. At approximately 9:00 AM, he was accompanied by Games officials to visit the sports field. Chu praised the construction of the Games venue, stating that the National Games could be held in Tianjin in the future. At noon, Zhang Boling accompanied him to Nankai to stay. Chu donated eight art pieces and three silver cups and shields to the Games.

Convenient Preferential Treatment for Postal, Telegraph, and Railway Services 155

The Tianjin Telegraph Bureau and Post Office set up temporary receiving and dispatching offices next to the front gate of the Games venue starting at 8:00 AM this morning to send and receive telegrams and letters. This newspaper reporter's telegram was sent from that office. The post office prepared special stamps for the Eighth Games as souvenirs. The Games organizing committee negotiated with the Beining Railway, offering a 25% discount on round-trip train tickets between Beiping and Tianjin from the 10th onwards for visitors.

Starting at 2:00 PM, there will be solo weapon performances and paired weapon performances, followed by wrestling matches. On the 13th, starting at 8:00 AM, there will be solo fist performances and paired fist performances. Starting at 2:00 PM, there will be solo weapon performances, wrestling double matches, and special skills demonstrations.

A joint meeting of all Games referees will be held at 9:00 AM on the 9th, convened by Chief Referee Zhang Boling. A meeting of all unit leaders and instructors will be held at 2:00 PM on the same afternoon, convened by Yuan Dunli. The grandstand is divided into sixteen sections, named after the phrases "Heaven and Earth are Black and Yellow," "The Universe is Vast and Wild," and "The Sun and Moon are Full and Waning, the Stars are Arranged in Order." Western Union First Division League

Jewish Team Crumbles; Yu You Achieves a Resounding 7-2 Victory 159

The disparity in strength allowed Yu You to consistently dominate.

In the final moments, the Jewish team conceded five consecutive goals.

Yesterday marked the first encounter between Central and Western teams in the Western Union First Division Football League. Yu You faced the Jewish team at Shen Garden. Having revamped their lineup, Yu You's strength was significantly enhanced, resulting in a crushing 7-2 victory over the newly promoted Jewish team. In the first half, the Jewish team, relying on their initial momentum, stubbornly resisted, resulting in a 1-1 tie. However, Yu You eventually took a 2-1 lead. In the second half, after going up 3-2, Yu You scored five consecutive goals, causing the Jewish team to crumble and suffer a crushing 7-2 defeat. Five to six thousand spectators watched and cheered, departing joyfully.

Jewish Technique Remains Immature

Yu You's handling of the

Jewish team yesterday can

be described as effortless,

consistently holding the

upper hand. Opportunities to score were numerous, but due to poor teamwork and unfamiliarity, the inability to coordinate led to countless missed chances, which is regrettable. Only Sun Jinshun and Luo Haiguang were able to score, while Zhong Yuxiang was completely unable to do so. The left wing was practically non-existent. Yu You's defense was decent, with Li Huiming being reliable and Yun Feng and Lie Mai putting in effort. Although Zhong Yongsen ran all over the field, the forward line felt uneven. As for the Jewish team, they possessed only courage, while their technique remained immature. The left wing of the forward line posed some danger.

Iron Leg Unleashes Power, Opening the Scoring

As the battle commenced, Yu

You kicked off. The Jewish

team fought desperately,

gritting their teeth and

repeatedly charging Yu You's defense. Li Huiguan commanded calmly, while Zuo Yun and Liang, the two generals, stubbornly guarded the gate, preventing any mishaps. Soon, Xiao Yun obtained a free-kick opportunity and passed it to South Seas star Zhong Yuxiang. Gao Erfei turned to intercept, but Zhong reacted swiftly, quickly lobbing it towards the center. Sun Jinshun, with lightning speed, shot the ball before it hit the ground, catching Dicklerek off guard and scoring a goal.

Mutual Exchange Concludes the First Half

The Jewish team, having suffered

this heavy blow, could not

endure it and sought

revenge. Pi Lingji took the

lead, leading his troops westward, but Li Huiguan ambushed him halfway, rendering his efforts futile. Pang Que sneaked into Yu You's penalty area, inviting Liang to charge. Pang passed the ball to L. Greenberg, who advanced like lightning and created a tie with a resounding shot. Seeing the danger, Luo Haiguang led his troops east, launching a solo attack, forcing a corner kick. Liang Shutang delivered the kick perfectly, allowing Luo Haiguang to head the ball in, making it 2-1 at the end of the first half.

Tit for Tat, Tense Situation In the second half, both

sides harbored the

ambition to win or die.

They attacked

and defended cautiously.

For ten minutes, no goals were scored. Suddenly, the opponent's right-wing forward advanced aggressively, leaving their defense vulnerable. Yang Mingjin was isolated and helpless, causing the spectators to worry. Fortunately, Wang Shusen rushed out from midfield, turning danger into safety. Sun Jinshun passed the ball well, allowing Xiao Luo to make a great contribution. Three minutes later, Xiao Yun regrettably touched the ball with his hand in the penalty area, resulting in a penalty kick. Henston, despite his age, succeeded with one attempt.

7-2, Like Crushing Eggs Against Stone In the blink of an eye, Xi

Aiqiao received orders

from Li's central army,

sent the word west, as

if entering a deserted land, passing it in front of the goal. Sun Jinshun tapped it in, recovering

lost ground. Not five minutes later, Luo Haiguang broke through the enemy's sentry line, entangled with old Henston. Sun's Iron Leg, taking advantage of the opponent's unpreparedness, forcefully shot the ball into the goal. Zhong Yongsen unleashed his pace and, seizing the opportunity, passed it to his clanmate, Yuxiang, who gently flicked it into the net. At this time, the Jewish team's morale was unstable, and the players were panic-stricken. The defenders looked disheartened. In a moment of exasperation, Xiao Luo fired a cannon from afar, hitting the bullseye again. Shortly after, the sun set, the shadows scattered, the victory was decided, and the order to retreat was given.

Third Yize Cup Youth Association Friendly Handball Ranking Tournament 163

Eighteen Participants Drawn for Positions

Competition Starts on the 11th of This Month

The Shanghai YMCA Sports Department has been promoting handball for several years, and there is an increasing number of members who love this game, resulting in a surge of talent, especially this year. The committee has decided that 18 people will participate in this ranking tournament, starting on the 11th of this month. It will take more than 150 matches to complete, with an estimated time of just over a month. The regulations and rankings are listed below:

(1) Sun Baoqi (2) Cai Tongshou (3) Lu Mengsheng (4) Ding Nayao (5) Gao Zishou (6) Huang Kesong (7) Sun Jialu (8) Zhu Kuan (9) Yuan Zongji (10) Zhai Zhenhu (11) Sun Daosheng (12) Yan Peiqiu (13) Hong Rulin (14) Hua Fenggang (15) Ma Xinyuan (16) Cheng Zhenhua (17) Yu Guanghan (18) Hong Yukui Regulations for the Third YMCA Ranking Cup Handball Tournament [Yize Cup] as follows: 1. This competition is named the [Yize Cup] Handball Ranking Tournament. The cup was donated by Mr. Cheng Yize.

2. Eight new players will participate in this competition. The qualifications for new players are determined by the Handball Committee.

3. The competition will adopt a [Promotion and Relegation System]. The starting positions will be determined by drawing lots.

4. Participants must arrive at the designated court at the designated time. Failure to arrive within five minutes of the scheduled time will result in a forfeit. However, exceptions can be made if the Sports Department agrees to a postponement one day prior to the match due to special circumstances. 5. The competition will adopt a best-of-three format, with each game to 21 points. (Note: If both sides reach 20 points, one side must score two more points to win.)

6. The competition is purely for honor and has no referees to judge the matches. Therefore, players are given a special opportunity to demonstrate their personal sportsmanship.

7. When serving or hitting the ball, if the ball touches the side wall and cannot be properly jumped, the serve should be re-served (Ground Rule).

8. Before the competition, players must first collect the competition report form and the ball from the shower room counter. After the competition, the result must be filled in and signed by both parties on the form to show seriousness, and then returned.

9. The competition ball will be provided by the Sports Department. Private balls cannot be used in the competition.

10. The results of the competition will be announced by the Sports Department the next day.

11. In order to particularly encourage the players, the following awards will be given:

A. The names of the top ten will be engraved on the Yize Cup as a permanent memorial.

B. The first place winner in this edition, excluding Mr. Zhu Kuan (himself), will donate a silver cup.

C. All those who maintain their original position (or improve) in the ranking competition for three consecutive years will each receive a silver shield from the department.

D. New players who reach the top ten in this edition will each receive a silver cup donated by Mr. Sun Daosheng.

Education News

Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education Reorganizes Education Funds in Various Counties 164

Organizing Education Fund Property Committees in Various Counties

Also Formulating Measures for Reorganizing Committees to Clean Up Education Funds

(Hangzhou Correspondence) Education fund property in various counties of Zhejiang Province has not been thoroughly investigated for a long time. The Department of Education previously issued orders to various counties to earnestly reorganize, but the results were not satisfactory. Now, the Department plans to organize a committee at the provincial level to be responsible for a thorough reorganization to increase the revenue of education funds in various counties. Ten articles of the regulations for the Zhejiang Provincial Education Fund Property Reorganization Committee have been drafted and passed by the Provincial Government Conference. The committee will be organized in the shortest possible time. The original regulations are recorded below: (Regulations for the Zhejiang Provincial Education Fund Property Reorganization Committee) Article 1: The Department of Education establishes the Education Fund Property Reorganization Committee to reorganize education fund property in various counties. Article 2: The members of this committee are organized by the Secretary of the Department of Education, the Chief of the relevant section, section staff, and all supervisors. Article 3: This committee has three standing committee members, designated by the Director of the Department of Education from among the committee members to oversee daily affairs and chair meetings on a rotating basis. Article 4: This committee is divided into two groups: Investigation and Cleaning. Each group has a director, appointed by the Director of the Department of Education from among the committee members. The duties of each group are as follows: 1. The Investigation Group investigates the situation of the funds in each county. 2. The Cleaning Group is dispatched to various counties to implement the cleaning. Article 5: This committee has one to two clerks, appointed by the Director of the Department of Education from among the clerks or secretaries in the department. Article 6: When cleaning up education fund property in various counties, if it is considered that the work cannot be handled by the personnel of this committee, specialists may be hired to assist in the handling. The salaries and travel expenses of the specialists shall be paid from the operating expenses of the Department of Education. Article 7: Measures for reorganizing committee members to clean up education fund property in various counties will be formulated separately. Article 8: The meetings of this committee are not held on a fixed date and are convened by the standing committee members at any time. Article 9: This committee is attached to the Department of Education. Article 10: These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Ministry of Education Cables Zhejiang to Investigate the Situation of Compensating for Education Expenses After Tax Reduction 165

Chairman Lu Orders the Departments of Finance and Education to Investigate and Reply

The Ministry of Education, in order to protect education, has issued repeated orders for action. Zhejiang Province abolished heavy taxes and miscellaneous levies on the 1st of this month. However, it is necessary to investigate whether the abolished taxes related to education have been compensated as ordered. A telegram was sent to Chairman Lu to inquire. The original telegram is recorded below: To Chairman Lu of the Hangzhou Provincial Government, With respect, How much is the total amount of education funds involved in your province's recent abolition of heavy taxes and miscellaneous levies? What are the compensation measures? Is there any impact on local education? Please order the relevant authorities to report in detail and expedite their response to the Ministry. This is greatly hoped for. Jiang, Ministry of Education. It is heard that Chairman Lu has ordered the two departments of finance and education to expedite their reply in order to forward it to the Ministry.

Zhejiang Provincial Government Orders Counties in the First School District to Raise and Distribute Education Funds as a Priority 166

The directors of the education bureaus of the counties in the first school district of Zhejiang Province stated that the education funds in their respective counties were in serious deficit. They requested the provincial government to order the county magistrates of various counties to raise and distribute education funds as a priority to maintain operations. After receiving the report, the provincial government considered that the dire financial situation of education in the counties of the school district was indeed the case. It approved the order to prioritize the raising and allocation of education funds. It is understood that orders have been issued to the county governments of various counties in the district to comply. As for the request to allocate provincial local government bonds, it has also been instructed to be handled after the bonds are issued.

Board of Directors of the China Educational Film Association 167

The third meeting of the third session of the Standing Committee of the China Educational Film Association was held in Beijing at 4:30 PM on the 6th. The Standing Committee members, the heads of the groups, and the yearbook editorial committee members Chen Lifu, Guo Youshou, Wu Yan Yin, Dai Ce, Wang Pingling, Lu Juewu, Li Jingbi, and Yang Minshi (Director of the Shanghai Branch) attended the meeting. Wu Yan Yin presided over the meeting (reporting matters): (1) The Hangzhou Branch reported on the process of its formal establishment. (2) The process of the Association's response to the Ministry of Education's order to review the letter from the Mexican Cultural Society regarding the production of films on history, archeology, and races. Society needs this kind of cultural work because the courses and schedules in schools are too fixed and inflexible. It is much nobler to use your spare time to study here than to do boring things, which waste time and energy. Reading a book always increases knowledge, which benefits not only individuals but also society and the nation. Therefore, from every perspective, we should support the reading group and hope that not only will the Youth Association continue to organize it this year, but that other places will also start organizing it, so that reading groups will flourish and expand day by day."

Special Article

The 1954 World Education Conference (3) 179

1. Establishment of a World Peace Committee to liaise with educational organizations in various countries, coordinate groups established in various countries around the world to achieve peace, and investigate and research effective and appropriate methods for achieving world peace through education. 2. A committee to investigate the current situation of history professors in the world. 3. A committee on international sports competitions. 4. A committee on mediation mechanisms. 5. A military education investigation committee. 6. A committee to investigate the theory that war is inevitable. 7. Establishment of a committee to investigate the relationship between the Hague Tribunal and the International Court of Justice and world education. Each committee will report the results of its investigations to the United Education Association, which will establish effective and appropriate strategies based on these reports.

The World United Education Association adopted this article at its first Edinburgh meeting. For the sake of convenience, five of the above-listed committees were attached to the Harman Charton Committee, namely: Part 1, Peace Education Department; Part 2, History Education Department; Part 3, International Sports Competition Department; Part 4, Military Education Department; Part 5, International Mediation Department. The departments of this committee will meet at each session. During the conferences of the general assembly, departments, and the Harman Charton Committee, educators from various countries around the world gather together to give speeches on various educational issues and report on the results of their investigations. In addition, representative conferences are held.

The representative conference is a conference composed of representatives from various countries and is the highest decision-making body in the World United Education Association. The election of directors, the determination of resolutions, and the amendment of constitutions and regulations are all carried out by the representative conference. The resolutions of each department and the Harman Charton Committee are organized by the resolution drafting committee, and the resolution of the World United Education Association is drafted, which is then reported to the representative conference. After being resolved by the representative conference, the resolution of the World United Education Association is formally published.

3. The 1935 World Education Conference and Japan. This World Education Conference will be held in Japan. Japanese educators believe that this conference is of great importance to Japan's great development during this extraordinary period. This can be explained from several aspects. In terms of international relations, since the "September 18th Incident," Japan has defied the world, abandoned its long-standing friendly facade, revealed its ferocious nature, brazenly occupied the three northeastern provinces, undermined world peace, violated the Nine-Power Treaty, and, during the "January 28th Incident," displayed its brutal bestiality in the prosperous

Shanghai. Ignoring everything, it resolutely withdrew from the League of Nations. In short, what Japan has shown to the world in recent years is nothing but the wild silkworm's habit of exhausting its resources in military expansion. The impression of Japan in Europe, America, and other parts of the world is entirely a picture of ferocity and greed. Moreover, Japan's diplomacy in recent years has often been in a state of isolation. Although Foreign Minister Hirota has recently advocated so-called "cooperative diplomacy," he has still been unable to break out of the isolated situation. This phenomenon is a great obstacle to Japan's national strength. In any case, Japan, because of the ambition of a few warlords, does not hesitate to be at odds with the world, which is the most foolish behavior. Therefore, the Japanese authorities, taking this into consideration, in order to shift the negative impressions of Japan held by Europeans and Americans, to avoid international disputes, and to break the international isolation, hope to use the most appropriate methods during this World Education Conference to carry out various propaganda activities, cover up Japan's ferocity and cruelty, and seek the understanding and sympathy of people from various countries. This is the diplomatic role that Japan hopes to play in the conference. (To be continued)

Free Talk

God's Chosen Sons 180

— Xiang Yu

I am not a narrow-minded person, but when I see the arrogant and domineering attitude of those people with high noses, green eyes, and blond hair, I always feel uncomfortable in my heart. I often wonder what they have to be proud of other than their high noses, green eyes, and blond hair. Stripped of the clothes they use to flaunt their gentlemanly manners, they are originally hairy people, and in terms of the degree of human evolution, they are at least two thousand years behind the Chinese. Leaving aside these gentlemen, and going further down the scale, to the sailors who come to China, we can often see conspicuous tattoos on their bodies - some are tattooed with anchors, some with men and women embracing - which is no different from the tattoos on the bodies of Chinese secret society members. If [tattooing] is a custom left over from savages, then how can these people, who see themselves as the most civilized, have savage customs? From the anthropological point of view, we must know that no matter how advanced a nation's culture is, there are still many remnants of barbarism from primitive times in its cultural characteristics. People with a broader vision and a fairer attitude will never deny a nation's entire culture simply because there are certain remnants of barbarism in that nation's culture. However, white people who come to the East are not like that. Their biased attitude and naive views are really annoying to see. They always think that they are God's chosen sons, and that their culture is also the most superior. As soon as they see that a certain cultural characteristic of China is different from theirs, they think it is either very mysterious or too barbaric.

Even in terms of eating, if you have been in contact with a white person for a long time, he will ask you with a curious and contemptuous tone: [Do Chinese people eat mice and snakes? Is this really the case]? If you are from Fujian or Guangdong and you answer yes, then he will simply be as if he has discovered a miracle, thinking that this is an incredible thing - if you are not from Fujian or Guangdong, and you answer him [I don't know, at least I don't eat them], then he simply considers you a liar, intentionally concealing the secrets of your country. We don't need to discuss the taste of snakes and mice, or whether they can or cannot be eaten. Even if eating snakes and mice is strange for people from Fujian and Guangdong, isn't eating snails by Europeans equally strange in the eyes of us Orientals?

Chinese food culture has its own standing and there is a definite conclusion about this. I remember a friend told me the following thing before (there is no doubt about the authenticity of this thing, maybe some exaggeration is inevitable): a few years ago, a few students from a certain university went to Germany to study. When the ship probably reached the Indian Ocean, it happened to be the Mid-Autumn Festival. Because the few students were tired of eating Western food, they wanted to eat Chinese food, so they went to the kitchen to discuss it, and asked to leave out a portion of raw chicken, fish, meat and vegetables for them to cook themselves. They cooked the dishes according to the Chinese method, the color was bright red, and the taste was also very good. The foreign cooks on the ship praised it greatly. In order to let the foreigners know the deliciousness of Chinese food, the few students specially left some for the cooks to eat. A fat, purulent head cook, who had just recovered from a minor illness, tore open a piece of chicken to taste it as soon as he saw the chicken dish with such good color. He discovered that Chinese food had a different flavor, so he ordered the other subordinates not to move and let him enjoy it alone. He also opened a few bottles of wine to help him enjoy it. After he was drunk and full and climbed onto a high bunk to sleep, whether he was too drunk or careless, he suddenly fell heavily from the bunk and broke his stomach and soon died.

The death of this head cook can prove the great magic power of Chinese food. China is at least no worse than others in terms of eating, but there are many people with high noses, green eyes, and blond hair who want to make trouble. I remember two years ago, a French reporter published an article in a famous foreign magazine saying that he was once invited by a Chinese person to dinner in Beijing. He felt that the house was too old, the cups and chopsticks were not clean enough, and the Chinese people's mixed eating habits were not in line with their customs. He thought that shark fins had no taste to speak of, so he felt that Chinese food had nothing to eat, and he used this as an excuse to rant and scold the Chinese. This kind of head facing big, ranting and raving, [farting, farting, really unreasonable] arrogant attitude. Are there only these kinds of things?

People who have traveled in Europe always feel that the blue-eyed people in Paris and Berlin are not as disgusting in their attitude as these people who come to the East. In fact, the attitude of these people who come to China is disgusting, and I am afraid that the Chinese have also cultivated half of it. The flattery of the compradors and foreign slaves is certainly enough to make them feel that they have suddenly risen a level. In addition, the so-called high-class Chinese in Shanghai welcome an inexplicable foreigner with particularly grand etiquette, which is also one of the reasons. A friend who came back from the United States once heard an American say to him: [White people in China are really God!] This is on the one hand a sign of the white people's pride, and on the other hand, it can be seen that the Chinese themselves are also to blame for the white people's pride.

Autumn 181

— Yingzi

Quietly, I picked up the diseased leaves brought down by the autumn wind and threw them into the tea stove; watching that spark of burning fire, I always had a feeling of waiting, as if I was hoping that a distant guest would come and chat with me while sipping tea. ...

Because I was a little sick, I had seven parts of leisure.

And these scattered days are not easy to have. People, probably always like to have a little leisure and fun, right? Although it is inevitably clear and chatty, but being quiet and peaceful is, after all, a good feeling for a heart that has been trampled on by life.

In order to covet the elegant and unrestrained beauty of the few parasol trees in the backyard, and the secluded location, I brought a set of tea sets and moved to this small study here to live. At the same time, I was also willing to be quietly in the study, savoring this rare tranquility.

[Parasol moon, pine breeze, banana rain, Tea stove, zither melody, sound of books]

Occasionally, I saw these two sentences on the tea canister and felt that they were quite similar to my situation today, so I asked someone to ask a calligrapher to write them and paste them on the wall. The gray wall was already decorated with many white spider nests.

Every day, I quietly brewed a pot of tea in such a scene with a feeling of waiting. ······

Time, also seemed to hang on the tail of a snail, so slowly, making people feel that it was not easy to wear away丨丨A sick and idle person probably has always experienced this feeling, right?

Especially, this situation makes people feel very empty.

The autumn wind was rustling from the parasol leaves. Outside the window, there was a curtain of quiet sunlight. When the wind passed, all sounds were silent, which I felt was some unbearable loneliness.

[Remember the small building,

Listening to the spring rain south of the Yangtze River all night,

Dreaming of the sound of the Xiao flute,

Flowing water, green duckweed,

Where is the old tour?]

When I silently recited the sentences of the lyricist Zhang Yutian in a tranquil and comfortable environment, I really didn't know where I was at this time. So, I often burned a furnace of good incense under the sunny window to savor [Legend] or [Ballad]. Leisurely, watching that wisp of rising green smoke, I would immerse my whole mind in the beautiful stories of love between men and women in those [Legends]. ······

At this time, the only thing that broke the silence was the sparse sound of tea in the stove.

And these simple and plain tones further intensified the silence of the surrounding air. At such times, I was often lost in thought, feeling that there was nothing to say.

On Naming Numbers 182

— Lengmo

The question I am raising is, the current numbering method is too cumbersome, how should it be reformed? I know that someone has proposed a reform method before, but it is still not very convenient, so I think it is best to create new characters. I have thought about it for a long time, and it seems that all four types of creation notes are possible. I am writing them out for everyone to study. If you think that one type is usable, I will be very happy. If all are rejected, then it is still one path. Below is the new proposed numbering table ··

Current Style: 个 十 百 千 万 十万 百万 十万万 百万万 千万万万 一百万万万万

Newly Proposed Characters: (Read Zhao) (Read Mi) (Read Di) (Read Qu)

Type A (From Ten): · · · Thousand (Or Dou) ·

Type B (From Thousand): · · · Thousand · · ·

Type C (From Ten Thousand): · · · · · · ·

Type D (From Zhao): · · · · · · · Billion Zhao Zhao

The last item in the current style, 百万万万万 (one hundred million million million), is obviously something that everyone finds unspeakable, but it is not an astronomical number, but is actually commonly used, i.e. Trillion in English and German, which can be used in statistics. What I am proposing here also ends with this word, but even larger ones can be inferred by analogy, because the proposed words all have a certain rule.

Type A is derived from IXON in Western science. Because the pronunciation of the original method is inconvenient and does not harmonize with the common concept of three-digit increments, it has been changed to a Chinese-style word and only takes three digits. Originally, K, O, etc. could be used directly, but it does not seem like a Chinese word and may be difficult to circulate. This type A is privately thought to be the most direct.

Type B is purely based on three increments (the square power of a thousand), and seems to be the easiest to write.

Type C relies on ten thousand increments, although it is slightly simpler, it is still cumbersome.

Type D can be said to be a translation of the Western numbering method. The word 兆 (Zhao) was used in the old ten thousand increment method to mean 十万万万 (one hundred million), but it was not widely used, so it still does not hinder it from being used as a million in the original decimal method; moreover, the phrase 四百兆 (四万万) 同胞 (four hundred million compatriots) is very popular, which helps its accuracy. This 兆 (Zhao) is equivalent to Lion in Western languages. I have not checked the etymology of the word Lion, but judging from the literal meaning, it seems to represent a number of one thousand times one thousand, so Million is one (Mi) one thousand times one thousand, Billion is the square of Lion (British and German methods are different, Trillion is the cube of Lion. Two words equivalent to it are created in Type D, and because Chinese is easy to combine, two words are created that are in between the three numbers. Further, the above can be inferred by analogy, or only Zhao increments can be used.

No matter which type is used, the pronunciation is proposed as above. 兆 (Zhao) is original, 密 (Mi) takes the first sound of the English and German word Milliardo, 蒂 (Di) takes the first sound of Billion, and 屈 (Qu) takes TriIIion. 蒂 (Di) then takes the changing sound of the word Thousand in 千乘兆兆 (thousand times Zhao times Zhao) or can read the ( ? ) proposed by Gao Mengdan.

Someone may answer that taking the sound of Western words is using Yi (foreigners) to change Xia (Chinese), but I feel that the most important thing about numbers is to show a clear concept. Instead of raising the sound of dead ancient words and making people confused, it is better to make many high school students and above understand the Western imagery and make it consistent. As for why only one sound is taken, one is for convenience, and the other is because the English and American meanings of the original word are different. Incomplete transliteration can avoid confusion. Third, meter is called 米 (Mi), and dozen is called 打 (Da). There are already precedents, and there is no inconvenience, so it can be imitated.

Scientists are the most courageous in creating new words, such as 气 (Qi), 腺 (Xian), etc. These words are good and convenient. The current arithmetic also clearly lacks a new word, and it is right to create a new word. I think this statement, at least scientists may not object.
